        Title = "Hello " .. LocalPlayer.Name .. "!",
        Content = "Welcome to Masteries Hub."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Before You Start",
        Content = "Would you like to bypass the anti-cheat?"
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Bypass All Anticheat",
        Description = "Attempts to bypass all anti-cheat systems.",
        Callback = function()
            loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/RobScripter/Slap-Battles/main/BypassAntiCheat.lua"))()
            task.wait(1.5)
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success",
                Content = "Bypassed All Anticheat",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Info About Mastery Gloves That Are Coming Soon...",
        Content = "The glove masteries that are coming soon are: (Obby, Run and Car Keys)"
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- INFO TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Info

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Info",
        Content = "Need a good executor to work properly."
    })

    -- Mastery Progress Tracker
    local player = LocalPlayer
    local playerGui = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")

    if playerGui:FindFirstChild("MasteryProgress") then
        playerGui.MasteryProgress:Destroy()
    end

    local hudGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    hudGui.Name = "MasteryProgress"
    hudGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
    hudGui.Parent = playerGui

    local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
    frame.Name = "TrackerOverlay"
    frame.Size = UDim2.fromOffset(340, 36)
    frame.Position = UDim2.fromOffset(40, 120)
    frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 35, 35)
    frame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.35
    frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    frame.Visible = true
    frame.Parent = hudGui

    local uiCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    uiCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6)
    uiCorner.Parent = frame

    local bar = Instance.new("Frame")
    bar.Name = "TopBar"
    bar.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 32)
    bar.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    bar.Parent = frame

    local titleLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    titleLabel.Name = "Title"
    titleLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    titleLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    titleLabel.Text = "Mastery Auto-Tracker"
    titleLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    titleLabel.TextSize = 16
    titleLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    titleLabel.Parent = bar

    local contentFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
    contentFrame.Name = "Content"
    contentFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, -32)
    contentFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 32)
    contentFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    contentFrame.Parent = frame

    local closeBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
    closeBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 24, 0, 24)
    closeBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -28, 0, 4)
    closeBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    closeBtn.Text = "X"
    closeBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
    closeBtn.TextSize = 18
    closeBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    closeBtn.Parent = bar

    local isTrackerActive = true

    closeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        isTrackerActive = false
        hudGui:Destroy()
    end)

    local masteryParagraph = nil

    local function updateParagraph(text)
        if masteryParagraph then
            pcall(function()
                masteryParagraph:SetDesc(text)
            end)
        end
    end

    local GloveMasteryClient
    task.spawn(function()
        local deps = game:GetService("ReplicatedFirst"):FindFirstChild("Dependencies")
        if deps then
            local mod = deps:FindFirstChild("GloveMasteryClient")
            if mod then
                pcall(function()
                    GloveMasteryClient = require(mod)
                end)
            end
        end
    end)

    local GLOVE_ALIASES = {
        ["Moai"] = "🗿",
        ["moai"] = "🗿",
        ["Moyai"] = "🗿"
    }

    local function getActiveGlove()
        local target = nil

        local ls = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
        if ls and ls:FindFirstChild("Glove") then
            local glove = ls.Glove.Value
            if glove and glove ~= "" and glove ~= "None" then
                target = glove
            end
        end

        if not target and player.Character then
            local tool = player.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
            if tool and tool.Name ~= "HumanoidRootPart" then
                target = tool.Name
            end
        end

        if not target then
            local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
            if backpack then
                local tool = backpack:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
                if tool then
                    target = tool.Name
                end
            end
        end

        if target and GLOVE_ALIASES[target] then
            return GLOVE_ALIASES[target], target
        end

        return target, target
    end

    local function isQuestCompleted(taskInfo)
        if taskInfo.Completed ~= nil then
            return taskInfo.Completed == true
        end

        local currentValue = tonumber(taskInfo.ProgressCurrent) or 0
        local maxValue = tonumber(taskInfo.ProgressMax) or 1

        return currentValue >= maxValue
    end

    local lastRenderedKey = ""

    local function renderOverlay(rows, currentGloveDisplay)
        local keyParts = { tostring(currentGloveDisplay or "Mastery") }
        for _, row in ipairs(rows) do
            table.insert(keyParts, tostring(row.quest) .. "|" .. tostring(row.progress) .. "|" .. tostring(row.completed))
        end

        local newKey = table.concat(keyParts, ";")
        if newKey == lastRenderedKey then return end
        lastRenderedKey = newKey

        for _, child in ipairs(contentFrame:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("TextLabel") then
                child:Destroy()
            end
        end

        local displayName = tostring(currentGloveDisplay or "Mastery")
        titleLabel.Text = displayName

        local count = #rows
        if count == 0 then
            frame.Size = UDim2.fromOffset(340, 32)
            updateParagraph("Glove Mastery: " .. displayName .. "\nNo active quests found.")
            return
        end

        local paragraphLines = {}
        table.insert(paragraphLines, "Glove Mastery: " .. displayName)

        for index, row in ipairs(rows) do
            local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            label.Name = "QuestRow"
            label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 44)
            label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, (index - 1) * 44)
            label.BackgroundTransparency = 1

            local progressText = row.progress or ""
            local completedText = row.completed and " ✅" or ""
            label.Text = tostring(row.quest or "") .. "\n" .. progressText .. completedText

            label.TextColor3 = row.completed and Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 100) or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            label.TextSize = 14
            label.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
            label.TextWrapped = true
            label.Parent = contentFrame

            table.insert(paragraphLines, "")
            table.insert(paragraphLines, "                    QUEST " .. index)
            table.insert(paragraphLines, "")
            table.insert(paragraphLines, "Description: " .. tostring(row.quest or ""))
            table.insert(paragraphLines, "Progress: " .. progressText .. (row.completed and " ✅" or ""))
        end

        frame.Size = UDim2.fromOffset(340, math.clamp(32 + count * 44, 60, 400))
        updateParagraph(table.concat(paragraphLines, "\n"))
    end

    local function renderStatus(title, message)
        if message == "" then
            renderOverlay({}, title or "Mastery")
            updateParagraph("Glove Mastery: " .. tostring(title or "Mastery") .. "\nNo data available.")
        else
            renderOverlay({ { quest = tostring(message or ""), progress = "", completed = false } }, title or "Mastery")
            updateParagraph("Glove Mastery: " .. tostring(title or "Mastery") .. "\n" .. tostring(message))
        end
    end

    local getthreadidentity = getthreadidentity or getthreadcontext or getidentity or function() return nil end
    local setthreadidentity = setthreadidentity or setthreadcontext or setidentity or function() end

    task.spawn(function()
        while isTrackerActive do
            task.wait()

            local internalGloveName, displayGloveName = getActiveGlove()

            if not internalGloveName then
                renderStatus("Mastery", "")
                continue
            end

            if not GloveMasteryClient then
                renderStatus("Mastery", "Loading data...")
                continue
            end

            local originalId = getthreadidentity()

            local s, parsedData = pcall(function()
                return GloveMasteryClient.GetMasteryChallengeProgresses(GloveMasteryClient, internalGloveName)
            end)

            if not s then
                s, parsedData = pcall(function()
                    return GloveMasteryClient.GetMasteryChallengeProgresses(internalGloveName)
                end)
            end

            if not s and displayGloveName ~= internalGloveName then
                s, parsedData = pcall(function()
                    return GloveMasteryClient.GetMasteryChallengeProgresses(displayGloveName)
                end)
            end

            if originalId then pcall(function() setthreadidentity(originalId) end) end

            if not s or type(parsedData) ~= "table" then
                renderOverlay({}, displayGloveName)
                continue
            end

            local rows = {}
            for _, taskInfo in ipairs(parsedData) do
                local taskName = taskInfo.Name or "Unknown Quest"
                local currentValue = tonumber(taskInfo.ProgressCurrent) or 0
                local maxValue = tonumber(taskInfo.ProgressMax) or 1
                local completed = isQuestCompleted(taskInfo)
                local percent = math.floor((currentValue / maxValue) * 100)

                local progressText = tostring(currentValue) .. " / " .. tostring(maxValue) .. " (" .. tostring(percent) .. "%)"

                table.insert(rows, {
                    quest = taskName,
                    progress = progressText,
                    completed = completed
                })
            end

            renderOverlay(rows, displayGloveName)
        end
    end)

    masteryParagraph = Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Glove Mastery Progress:",
        Content = "Loading..."
    })

    hudGui.Enabled = false
    frame.Visible = false
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- OTHER STUFF TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.OtherStuff

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Give FE/Visual Free Mastery",
        Content = "Select a glove and apply mastery visual."
    })

    local masteryNames = {
        "spin", "Stick", "Brick", "Flash", "Spring", "Pinwheel", "Dice", "Thanos", "Fort", "Space", "Hive", "Mace", "Killstreak", "Gummy",
        "Engineer", "Phantom", "Wormhole", "Stalker", "Cherry", "Booster", "BONK", "Cloud", "Soul",
        "[REDACTED]", "bus", "Phase", "Bomb", "Bubble", "Shard", "Moon", "Rage", "Chain", "Tycoon",
        "🗿", "Obby", "Voodoo", "rob", "Tinkerer", "Glovel", "Firework", "Run", "Frostbite", "Plank", "Hexa", "Eggler", "Car Keys",
        "Ultra Instinct", "Acrobat"
    }

    local selectedMastery = masteryNames[1]
    local hookfunctionSupported = pcall(function() return hookfunction end)

    local Dropdown = Tab:AddDropdown("MasterySelect", {
        Title = "Select Glove for Mastery",
        Description = "Choose a glove to apply visual mastery.",
        Values = masteryNames,
        Multi = false,
        Default = 1,
        Callback = function(Value)
            selectedMastery = Value
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Apply Mastery",
        Description = "Applies visual mastery to the selected glove.",
        Callback = function()
            if not hookfunctionSupported then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Your executor doesn't support hookfunction",
                    Duration = 5
                })
                return
            end

            local success, err = pcall(function()
                local mod = require(game.ReplicatedFirst.Dependencies.GloveMasteryClient)
                local old = mod.IsMasteredVersionEnabled
                hookfunction(mod.IsMasteredVersionEnabled, function(self, g)
                    return g == selectedMastery or old(self, g)
                end)
            end)

            if success then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Success",
                    Content = selectedMastery .. " mastery applied!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Failed to apply mastery: " .. tostring(err),
                    Duration = 3
                })
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Warning",
                    Content = "Your executor doesn't support hookfunction",
                    Duration = 5
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Main Stuff",
        Content = ""
    })

    local anchorEnabled = false
    Tab:AddToggle("AnchorSelf", {
        Title = "Anchor Yourself",
        Description = "Anchors your character's head in place.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            anchorEnabled = Value
            if Value then
                local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                if char then
                    local head = char:FindFirstChild("Head")
                    if head then
                        head.Anchored = true
                    end
                end
            else
                local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                if char then
                    local head = char:FindFirstChild("Head")
                    if head then
                        head.Anchored = false
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    })

    local autoDieOnRagdoll = false
    Tab:AddToggle("AutoDieOnRagdoll", {
        Title = "Auto Die On Ragdoll",
        Description = "Automatically kills you when ragdolled.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoDieOnRagdoll = Value
            if Value then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while autoDieOnRagdoll do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                                if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                    local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                                    if humanoid then
                                        humanoid.Health = 0
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Normal Arena Portal",
        Description = "Teleports you to the normal arena portal.",
        Callback = function()
            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
            if char then
                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if hrp then
                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                end
            end
        end
    })

    local autoPortal = false
    local portalLoop = nil
    Tab:AddToggle("AutoPortalTeleport", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Normal Arena Portal",
        Description = "Continuously teleports to the normal arena portal.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoPortal = Value
            if Value then
                if portalLoop then
                    task.cancel(portalLoop)
                    portalLoop = nil
                end
                portalLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoPortal do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
            else
                if portalLoop then
                    task.cancel(portalLoop)
                    portalLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Normal Safespot Stuff",
        Content = ""
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Create Normal Safespot",
        Description = "Creates a safespot in the void.",
        Callback = function()
            if workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot") == nil then
                local Safespot = Instance.new("Model", workspace)
                Safespot.Name = "Safespot"

                local base = Instance.new("Part")
                base.Name = "Base"
                base.Size = Vector3.new(500, 10, 500)
                base.Position = Vector3.new(10000, -50, 10000)
                base.Anchored = true
                base.CanCollide = true
                base.Transparency = 0.5
                base.Parent = Safespot

                local partsData = {
                    {"DefendPart",  Vector3.new(500, 117, 5),   Vector3.new(10000.2, 13, 9752.45)},
                    {"DefendPart1", Vector3.new(5, 117, 496),   Vector3.new(10248.2, 13, 10002.4)},
                    {"DefendPart2", Vector3.new(497, 117, 6),   Vector3.new(9998.13, 13, 10247.2)},
                    {"DefendPart3", Vector3.new(7, 117, 490),   Vector3.new(9752.71, 13, 9999.28)},
                    {"DefendPart4", Vector3.new(491, 10, 491),  Vector3.new(10001.1, 76, 9999.66)},
                }

                for _, partInfo in pairs(partsData) do
                    local part = Instance.new("Part")
                    part.Name = partInfo[1]
                    part.Size = partInfo[2]
                    part.Position = partInfo[3]
                    part.Anchored = true
                    part.CanCollide = true
                    part.Transparency = 0.5
                    part.Parent = Safespot
                end

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Success",
                    Content = "Safespot Created Successfully!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot already exists!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Destroy/Delete Normal Safespot",
        Description = "Deletes the normal safespot.",
        Callback = function()
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if safespot then
                safespot:Destroy()
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Done",
                    Content = "Safespot Destroyed/Deleted Successfully!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot Not Found",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Normal Safespot",
        Description = "Teleports you to the normal safespot.",
        Callback = function()
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if safespot then
                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                if base then
                    local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                    if char then
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if hrp then
                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                        end
                    end
                end
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Create Safespot first!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    local autoSafespot = false
    local safespotLoop = nil
    Tab:AddToggle("AutoNormalSafespot", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Normal Safespot",
        Description = "Continuously teleports to the normal safespot.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoSafespot = Value
            if Value then
                if safespotLoop then
                    task.cancel(safespotLoop)
                    safespotLoop = nil
                end
                safespotLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoSafespot do
                        pcall(function()
                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                                    if char then
                                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if hrp then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
            else
                if safespotLoop then
                    task.cancel(safespotLoop)
                    safespotLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Cloud Only Safespot Stuff",
        Content = ""
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Create Cloud Safespot",
        Description = "Creates a safespot in the cloud area.",
        Callback = function()
            if workspace:FindFirstChild("CloudSafespot") == nil then
                local CloudSafespot = Instance.new("Model", workspace)
                CloudSafespot.Name = "CloudSafespot"

                local centerPos = Vector3.new(-4522, 64, -223)

                local base = Instance.new("Part")
                base.Name = "Base"
                base.Size = Vector3.new(500, 10, 500)
                base.Position = centerPos
                base.Anchored = true
                base.CanCollide = true
                base.Transparency = 0.5
                base.Parent = CloudSafespot

                local halfSize = 250
                local wallHeight = 117
                local wallThickness = 5

                local frontWall = Instance.new("Part")
                frontWall.Name = "DefendPart"
                frontWall.Size = Vector3.new(500, wallHeight, wallThickness)
                frontWall.Position = centerPos + Vector3.new(0, wallHeight/2 + 5, halfSize)
                frontWall.Anchored = true
                frontWall.CanCollide = true
                frontWall.Transparency = 0.5
                frontWall.Parent = CloudSafespot

                local backWall = Instance.new("Part")
                backWall.Name = "DefendPart1"
                backWall.Size = Vector3.new(500, wallHeight, wallThickness)
                backWall.Position = centerPos + Vector3.new(0, wallHeight/2 + 5, -halfSize)
                backWall.Anchored = true
                backWall.CanCollide = true
                backWall.Transparency = 0.5
                backWall.Parent = CloudSafespot

                local rightWall = Instance.new("Part")
                rightWall.Name = "DefendPart2"
                rightWall.Size = Vector3.new(wallThickness, wallHeight, 500)
                rightWall.Position = centerPos + Vector3.new(halfSize, wallHeight/2 + 5, 0)
                rightWall.Anchored = true
                rightWall.CanCollide = true
                rightWall.Transparency = 0.5
                rightWall.Parent = CloudSafespot

                local leftWall = Instance.new("Part")
                leftWall.Name = "DefendPart3"
                leftWall.Size = Vector3.new(wallThickness, wallHeight, 500)
                leftWall.Position = centerPos + Vector3.new(-halfSize, wallHeight/2 + 5, 0)
                leftWall.Anchored = true
                leftWall.CanCollide = true
                leftWall.Transparency = 0.5
                leftWall.Parent = CloudSafespot

                local roof = Instance.new("Part")
                roof.Name = "DefendPart4"
                roof.Size = Vector3.new(491, 10, 491)
                roof.Position = centerPos + Vector3.new(0, wallHeight + 10 + 5, 0)
                roof.Anchored = true
                roof.CanCollide = true
                roof.Transparency = 0.5
                roof.Parent = CloudSafespot

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Success",
                    Content = "Cloud Safespot Created Successfully!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Cloud Safespot already exists!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Destroy/Delete Cloud Safespot",
        Description = "Deletes the cloud safespot.",
        Callback = function()
            local CloudSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("CloudSafespot")
            if CloudSafespot then
                CloudSafespot:Destroy()
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Done",
                    Content = "Cloud Safespot Destroyed/Deleted Successfully!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Cloud Safespot Not Found",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Cloud Safespot",
        Description = "Teleports you to the cloud safespot.",
        Callback = function()
            local CloudSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("CloudSafespot")
            if CloudSafespot then
                local base = CloudSafespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                if base then
                    local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                    if char then
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if hrp then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(base.Position + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0))
                        end
                    end
                end
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Create Cloud Safespot first!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    local autoCloudSafespot = false
    local CloudsafespotLoop = nil
    Tab:AddToggle("AutoCloudSafespot", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Cloud Safespot",
        Description = "Continuously teleports to the cloud safespot.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoCloudSafespot = Value

            if Value then
                if CloudsafespotLoop then
                    task.cancel(CloudsafespotLoop)
                    CloudsafespotLoop = nil
                end

                CloudsafespotLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoCloudSafespot do
                        pcall(function()
                            local CloudSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("CloudSafespot")
                            if CloudSafespot then
                                local base = CloudSafespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                    if char then
                                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if hrp then
                                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(base.Position + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0))
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
            else
                if CloudsafespotLoop then
                    task.cancel(CloudsafespotLoop)
                    CloudsafespotLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Misc Stuff",
        Content = ""
    })

    local antiAfkEnabled = false
    Tab:AddToggle("AntiAFK", {
        Title = "Anti AFK",
        Description = "Prevents you from being kicked for being AFK.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            antiAfkEnabled = Value
            if Value then
                LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                    VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                    VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
                end)
            end
        end
    })

    local antiRagdollEnabled = false
    Tab:AddToggle("AntiRagdoll", {
        Title = "Anti Ragdoll",
        Description = "Prevents you from being ragdolled.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            antiRagdollEnabled = Value

            if antiRagdollEnabled then
                task.spawn(function()
                    local lastCFrame = nil
                    local lastPosition = nil
                    local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                    local humanoidRootPart = nil

                    while antiRagdollEnabled do
                        pcall(function()
                            character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if not character then
                                task.wait(0.1)
                                return
                            end

                            humanoidRootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local ragdolledValue = character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")

                            if humanoidRootPart and (not ragdolledValue or ragdolledValue.Value == false) then
                                lastCFrame = humanoidRootPart.CFrame
                                lastPosition = humanoidRootPart.Position
                            end

                            if ragdolledValue and ragdolledValue.Value == true and lastCFrame and humanoidRootPart then
                                humanoidRootPart.CFrame = lastCFrame
                                humanoidRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                                humanoidRootPart.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)

                                for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                                    if part:IsA("BasePart") and part ~= humanoidRootPart then
                                        part.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                                        part.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                                    end
                                end

                                local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                if humanoid then
                                    humanoid.PlatformStand = false
                                    humanoid.Sit = false
                                end

                                task.wait()
                                if character and character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") then
                                    character.Ragdolled.Value = false
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait()
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Anti Ragdoll",
                    Content = "Enabled! Instant ragdoll prevention.",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })
end

do
    local Tab = Tabs.Spin

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Spin on the Slap Battles Logo"
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Safespot",
        Description = "Teleports you to the safespot for Spin mastery.",
        Callback = function()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local character = player.Character

            local hasSpinGlove = player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "spin"
            local hasEntered = character and character:FindFirstChild("entered")
            local hasSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")

            if not hasSpinGlove or not hasEntered or not hasSafespot then
                local errorMsg = ""
                if not hasSpinGlove then
                    errorMsg = "Equip Spin Glove"
                elseif not hasEntered then
                    errorMsg = "Enter Arena First"
                elseif not hasSafespot then
                    errorMsg = "Create Safespot First"
                end

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return
            end

            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if safespot then
                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                if base then
                    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if hrp then
                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)

                        Fluent:Notify({
                            Title = "Teleported",
                            Content = "Teleported to Safespot!",
                            Duration = 2
                        })
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

-- STICK TAB

do
    local Tab = Tabs.Stick

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Stick to someone"
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Stick mastery."
    })

    local autoSafespotStick = false
    local safespotLoopStick = nil
    local slapAuraConnectionStick = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("StickReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoSafespotStick = Value

            if Value then
                if safespotLoopStick then
                    task.cancel(safespotLoopStick)
                    safespotLoopStick = nil
                end

                safespotLoopStick = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoSafespotStick do
                        pcall(function()
                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                    if char then
                                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if hrp then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                if slapAuraConnectionStick then
                    slapAuraConnectionStick:Disconnect()
                    slapAuraConnectionStick = nil
                end

                slapAuraConnectionStick = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                    if not autoSafespotStick then return end

                    pcall(function()
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if not generalHit then return end

                        for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                            if player.Character then
                                local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if targetPart then
                                    generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Safespot + Slap Aura",
                    Content = "Enabled! Teleporting to Safespot & slapping all players.",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if safespotLoopStick then
                    task.cancel(safespotLoopStick)
                    safespotLoopStick = nil
                end

                if slapAuraConnectionStick then
                    slapAuraConnectionStick:Disconnect()
                    slapAuraConnectionStick = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Stick mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverSafespotStick = false
    local receiverSafespotLoopStick = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("StickHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot (Receiver)",
        Description = "Teleports to the safespot for the receiver role.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverSafespotStick = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverSafespotStick = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverSafespotLoopStick then
                    task.cancel(receiverSafespotLoopStick)
                    receiverSafespotLoopStick = nil
                end

                receiverSafespotLoopStick = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverSafespotStick do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Teleport",
                    Content = "Auto teleport to Safespot (Receiver) enabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })

            else
                if receiverSafespotLoopStick then
                    task.cancel(receiverSafespotLoopStick)
                    receiverSafespotLoopStick = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

do
    local Tab = Tabs.Brick

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Brick Master"
    })

    local brickMasterRunning = false
    local brickMasterLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("BrickMaster", {
        Title = "Auto Obtain Brick Master Badge",
        Description = "Automatically obtains the Brick Master badge.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            if Value then
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

                local hasBrickGlove = player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Brick"
                local hasEntered = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("entered")
                local hasSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")

                if not hasBrickGlove or not hasEntered or not hasSafespot then
                    local errorMsg = ""
                    if not hasBrickGlove then
                        errorMsg = "Equip Brick Glove"
                    elseif not hasEntered then
                        errorMsg = "Enter Arena First"
                    elseif not hasSafespot then
                        errorMsg = "Create Safespot First"
                    end

                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = errorMsg,
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    return false
                end

                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if safespot then
                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                    if base then
                        local hrp = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if hrp then
                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                        end
                    end
                end

                task.wait(0.5)

                getgenv().BrickMasterLoop = true
                brickMasterLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while getgenv().BrickMasterLoop do
                        pcall(function()
                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                    if char then
                                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if hrp then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local lbrick = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("lbrick")
                            if lbrick then
                                lbrick:FireServer()
                            end

                            pcall(function()
                                local gui = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("BRICKCOUNT")
                                if gui then
                                    local imageLabel = gui:FindFirstChild("ImageLabel")
                                    if imageLabel then
                                        local textLabel = imageLabel:FindFirstChild("TextLabel")
                                        if textLabel then
                                            local currentCount = tonumber(textLabel.Text) or 0
                                            textLabel.Text = tostring(currentCount + 1)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end)
                        end)
                        task.wait(1.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Brick Master",
                    Content = "Auto Obtain Brick Master Badge Started!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                getgenv().BrickMasterLoop = false
                if brickMasterLoop then
                    task.cancel(brickMasterLoop)
                    brickMasterLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "2-4 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 1K Bricks, Brick Block, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",

                    })
                    autoReceiverSafespotBrick = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverSafespotLoopBrick then
                    task.cancel(receiverSafespotLoopBrick)
                    receiverSafespotLoopBrick = nil

                    while autoReceiverSafespotBrick do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character

                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

                                    local targetPart = nil
                                    for _, part in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                        if part:IsA("Part") and part.Name == "Union" then
                                            if part.Size.X == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.X and
                                                part.Size.Y == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.Y and
                                                part.Size.Z == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.Z then
                                                targetPart = part
                                                break
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end

                                    if targetPart then
                                        hrp.CFrame = targetPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                    else
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Teleport",
                    Content = "Auto teleport to Safespot/Bricks enabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })

            else
                if receiverSafespotLoopBrick then
                    task.cancel(receiverSafespotLoopBrick)
                    receiverSafespotLoopBrick = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "3 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Brick Block"
    })

    Tab:AddToggle("BrickFling", {
        Title = "Auto Fling Bricks",
        Description = "Fling bricks around you.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            if Value then
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

                if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value ~= "Brick" then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Equip Brick Glove first!",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    return false
                end

                local TARGET_UNION_SIZE = Vector3.new(1.3293739557266235, 0.4905083179473877, 0.8358331918716431)

                getgenv().UnionsFlingLoop = true

                task.spawn(function()
                    local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
                    local speaker = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                    local flinging = true

                    local noclipConnection
                    noclipConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
                        if speaker.Character then
                            for _, part in pairs(speaker.Character:GetDescendants()) do
                                if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.CanCollide then
                                    part.CanCollide = false
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)

                    local function onCharacterAdded(char)
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
                        if humanoid then
                            humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                                flinging = false
                                if noclipConnection then
                                    noclipConnection:Disconnect()
                                end
                                getgenv().UnionsFlingLoop = false
                            end)
                        end
                    end

                    local humanoid = speaker.Character and speaker.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
                    if humanoid then
                        humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                            flinging = false
                            if noclipConnection then
                                noclipConnection:Disconnect()
                            end
                            getgenv().UnionsFlingLoop = false
                        end)
                    end

                    speaker.CharacterAdded:Connect(onCharacterAdded)

                    while getgenv().UnionsFlingLoop and flinging do
                        RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
                        local character = speaker.Character
                        local root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local vel, movel = nil, 0.1

                        while not (character and character.Parent and root and root.Parent) do
                            RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
                            character = speaker.Character
                            root = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        end

                        vel = root.Velocity
                        root.Velocity = vel * 10000 + Vector3.new(0, 10000, 0)

                        RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
                        if character and character.Parent and root and root.Parent then
                            root.Velocity = vel
                        end

                        RunService.Stepped:Wait()
                        if character and character.Parent and root and root.Parent then
                            root.Velocity = vel + Vector3.new(0, movel, 0)
                            movel = movel * -1
                        end

                        for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                            if obj:IsA("BasePart") and obj.Name == "Union" then
                                if obj.Size.X == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.X and
                                    obj.Size.Y == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.Y and
                                    obj.Size.Z == TARGET_UNION_SIZE.Z then
                                    pcall(function()
                                        local originalCFrame = obj.CFrame
                                        local originalAnchored = obj.Anchored

                                        obj.Anchored = false
                                        obj.CFrame = root.CFrame
                                        task.wait(0.01)
                                        obj.CFrame = originalCFrame
                                        obj.Anchored = originalAnchored
                                    end)
                                end
                            end
                        end

                        task.wait(0.05)
                    end

                    if noclipConnection then
                        noclipConnection:Disconnect()
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Fling Bricks",
                    Content = "Enabled! Flinging and bringing Unions.",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                getgenv().UnionsFlingLoop = false
            end
        end
    })
end

do
    local Tab = Tabs.Flash

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-3 Quest",

    })

        Title = "Auto Use Ability (Instant But Kicks)",
        Description = "Uses Flash ability 1500 times instantly.",
        Callback = function()
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Flash" then
                for i = 1, 1500 do
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("FlashTeleport"):FireServer()
                    task.wait()
                end
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Flash Glove",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "2 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Kill 150 Players With Flash"
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Flash mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperSafespotFlash = false
    local helperSafespotLoopFlash = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("FlashReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperSafespotFlash = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperSafespotFlash = false
                    return
                end

                if helperSafespotLoopFlash then
                    task.cancel(helperSafespotLoopFlash)
                    helperSafespotLoopFlash = nil
                end

                helperSafespotLoopFlash = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperSafespotFlash do
                        pcall(function()
                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                    if char then
                                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if hrp then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local flashTeleport = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("FlashTeleport")
                            if flashTeleport then
                                flashTeleport:FireServer()
                            end

                            task.wait(3)

                            local flashHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("FlashHit")
                            if flashHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            flashHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperSafespotLoopFlash then
                    task.cancel(helperSafespotLoopFlash)
                    helperSafespotLoopFlash = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Flash mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverTeleportFlash = false
    local receiverTeleportLoopFlash = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("FlashHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
        Description = "Teleports to the receiver position.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverTeleportFlash = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverTeleportFlash = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverTeleportLoopFlash then
                    task.cancel(receiverTeleportLoopFlash)
                    receiverTeleportLoopFlash = nil
                end

                receiverTeleportLoopFlash = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverTeleportFlash do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver Teleport",
                    Content = "Auto teleport to Receiver position enabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })

            else
                if receiverTeleportLoopFlash then
                    task.cancel(receiverTeleportLoopFlash)
                    receiverTeleportLoopFlash = nil

            end

    })

-- PINWHEEL TAB

do
    local Tab = Tabs.Pinwheel

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Kill 500 Players with Pinwheel, Hit 1K Players with Pinwheel, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Pinwheel mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverPinwheel = false
    local receiverLoopThreadPinwheel = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("PinwheelReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverPinwheel = Value

            if Value then
                if receiverLoopThreadPinwheel then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadPinwheel)
                    receiverLoopThreadPinwheel = nil
                end

                receiverLoopThreadPinwheel = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverPinwheel do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then return end

                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                            if generalAbility then
                                generalAbility:FireServer()
                            end
                            task.wait(1)

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local startTime = tick()
                                while autoReceiverPinwheel and (tick() - startTime) < 0.5 do
                                    pcall(function()
                                        for _, targetPlayer in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                            if targetPlayer.Character then
                                                local targetParts = {
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm"),
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm"),
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head"),
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso"),
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"),
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("DOLLPART")
                                                }

                                                for _, part in pairs(targetParts) do
                                                    if part then
                                                        generalHit:FireServer(part)
                                                    end
                                                end
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end)
                                    task.wait(1)
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Receiver Enabled! (Safespot + Ability + Slap Aura)",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverLoopThreadPinwheel then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadPinwheel)
                    receiverLoopThreadPinwheel = nil
                end

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Receiver Disabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Pinwheel mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperPinwheel = false
    local helperLoopThreadPinwheel = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("PinwheelHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll + Auto Enter Arena",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver, dies on ragdoll, and enters arena.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperPinwheel = Value

            if Value then
                if helperLoopThreadPinwheel then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopThreadPinwheel)
                    helperLoopThreadPinwheel = nil
                end

                helperLoopThreadPinwheel = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperPinwheel do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then return end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(1)
                                hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                            end
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                Fluent:Notify({
                                    Title = "Ragdoll",
                                    Content = "Died due to ragdoll!",
                                    Duration = 2
                                })
                                task.wait(1)
                                return
                            end

                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Helper Enabled! (Receiver + Die On Ragdoll + Enter Arena)",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperLoopThreadPinwheel then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopThreadPinwheel)
                    helperLoopThreadPinwheel = nil
                end

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Helper Disabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })
end

        Default = false,

                    while autoHelperFullDice do

                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

                                return
                            end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then

                                if billboard then
                                    local imageLabel = billboard:FindFirstChild("ImageLabel")
                                    if imageLabel then
                                        local textLabel = imageLabel:FindFirstChild("TextLabel")
                                        if textLabel then
                                            local text = textLabel.Text
                                            local number = tonumber(text)
                                            if number and number >= 60 then
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end

                Fluent:Notify({

                    Duration = 3
