-- =================================================================================================
-- THANOS TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Thanos

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Kill 25 Players With Thanos, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Thanos mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverFullThanos = false
    local receiverFullLoopThanos = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("ThanosReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura + Auto Use Ability",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, slaps all players, and uses ability.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverFullThanos = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverFullThanos = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverFullLoopThanos then
                    task.cancel(receiverFullLoopThanos)
                    receiverFullLoopThanos = nil
                end

                receiverFullLoopThanos = task.spawn(function()
                    local abilityTimer = 0

                    while autoReceiverFullThanos do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            abilityTimer = abilityTimer + 0.5
                            if abilityTimer >= 3 then
                                abilityTimer = 0
                                local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                                if generalAbility then
                                    generalAbility:FireServer(2)
                                end
                            end

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura + Ability Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverFullLoopThanos then
                    task.cancel(receiverFullLoopThanos)
                    receiverFullLoopThanos = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Thanos mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperSlapThanos = false
    local helperSlapLoopThanos = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("ThanosHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperSlapThanos = Value

            if Value then
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                local glove = player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if not glove or glove.Value ~= "Default" then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Equip Default Glove first!",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperSlapThanos = false
                    return
                end

                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperSlapThanos = false
                    return
                end

                if helperSlapLoopThanos then
                    task.cancel(helperSlapLoopThanos)
                    helperSlapLoopThanos = nil
                end

                helperSlapLoopThanos = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperSlapThanos do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    else
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local bRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("b")
                            if bRemote then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            bRemote:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({

                    Duration = 3

-- =================================================================================================
-- FORT TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Fort

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Fort Badge"
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Get Badge + Plank Glove",
        Description = "Obtains the Fort badge and Plank glove.",
        Callback = function()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Fort" and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                local hrp = player.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                local originalPos = hrp.CFrame

                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(8, 97, 4)
                wait(0.2)
                hrp.Anchored = true
                wait(0.3)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Fortlol:FireServer()
                wait(3.5)
                hrp.Anchored = false
                wait(0.1)
                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(8, 106, -6)
                wait(0.5)
                hrp.CFrame = originalPos
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Fort Glove/Enter Arena",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with Fort, etc."
    })

    local autoFortDestroy = false
    local fortDestroyLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("FortDestroy", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Auto Destroy Fort Walls",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and destroys fort walls.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoFortDestroy = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoFortDestroy = false
                    return
                end

                if fortDestroyLoop then
                    task.cancel(fortDestroyLoop)
                    fortDestroyLoop = nil
                end

                fortDestroyLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoFortDestroy do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not hrp then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local fortlol = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Fortlol")
                            if fortlol then
                                fortlol:FireServer()
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local targetPart = nil
                            local targetColor = Color3.fromRGB(172, 73, 73)

                            for _, part in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.Name == "Part" then
                                    local partColor = part.Color
                                    if partColor.R == targetColor.R and
                                        partColor.G == targetColor.G and
                                        partColor.B == targetColor.B then
                                        targetPart = part
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            if targetPart then
                                hrp.CFrame = targetPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)

                                task.wait(0.3)

                                local selfKnockback = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("SelfKnockback")
                                if selfKnockback then
                                    selfKnockback:FireServer({
                                        Force = 0,
                                        Direction = Vector3.new(0, 0.01, 0)
                                    })
                                end
                            end
                        end)

                        task.wait(4)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Fort Destroy",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Destroy Fort Walls Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if fortDestroyLoop then
                    task.cancel(fortDestroyLoop)
                    fortDestroyLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

-- SPACE TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Space

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "2 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Use Bus"
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Someone Using bus?",
        Description = "Checks if someone is using the Bus glove.",
        Callback = function()
            local found = false

            for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
                local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if leaderstats then
                    local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                    if glove and glove.Value == "bus" then
                        found = true
                        Fluent:Notify({
                            Title = "Detected!",
                            Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the bus glove.",
                            Duration = 3
                        })
                    end
                end
            end

            if not found then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "No one has equipped the bus glove",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To bus Player",
        Description = "Teleports to the nearest bus glove user.",
        Callback = function()
            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local foundPlayer = nil

            for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= localPlayer then
                    local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                    if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "bus" then
                        foundPlayer = player
                        break
                    end
                end
            end

            if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Success!",
                    Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                    Duration = 3
                })
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "bus Player Not Found",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    local Giftfarm = false
    Tab:AddToggle("SpaceBusBring", {
        Title = "Auto Bring Bus",
        Description = "Brings the bus model to you.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            Giftfarm = Value

            task.spawn(function()
                while Giftfarm do
                    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                    if not player then
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        continue
                    end

                    local character = player.Character
                    if not character or not character.Parent then
                        task.wait(0.01)
                        continue
                    end

                    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if not hrp then
                        task.wait(0.01)
                        continue
                    end

                    for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                        if v.Name == "BusModel" and v:IsA("MeshPart") then
                            pcall(function()
                                local originalCFrame = v.CFrame
                                local originalAnchored = v.Anchored

                                for _, child in pairs(v:GetChildren()) do
                                    if child:IsA("TouchInterest") then
                                        child:Destroy()
                                    end
                                end

                                v.Anchored = false
                                v.CFrame = hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 0, 5)
                                task.wait(0.05)
                            end)
                        end
                    end

                    task.wait(0.05)
                end
            end)
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "3 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Get Slapple"
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Cannon Island",
        Description = "Teleports to Cannon Island.",
        Callback = function()
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Space" then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(229, 47, 170)
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Space Glove",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Slapple Island",
        Description = "Teleports to Slapple Island.",
        Callback = function()
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Space" then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-389, 51, -23)
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Space Glove",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-4 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 1K Players with Space, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Space mastery."
    })

    local receiverAbilitySlapLoopSpace = nil

                    receiverBarrierLoop = nil
                end

                receiverBarrierLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverBarrier do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local barrier = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Barrier")
                            if barrier then
                                barrier:FireServer(1)
                            end

                            task.wait(0.01)

                            local defenseHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("DefenseHit")
                            if defenseHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            defenseHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Barrier + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverBarrierLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverBarrierLoop)
                    receiverBarrierLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Defense mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperReceiverTeleport2 = false
    local helperReceiverTeleportLoop2 = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("DefenseHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
        Description = "Teleports to the receiver position.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperReceiverTeleport2 = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperReceiverTeleport2 = false
                    return
                end

                if helperReceiverTeleportLoop2 then
                    task.cancel(helperReceiverTeleportLoop2)
                    helperReceiverTeleportLoop2 = nil
                end

                helperReceiverTeleportLoop2 = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperReceiverTeleport2 do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    else
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto teleport to Receiver position enabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })

            else
                if helperReceiverTeleportLoop2 then
                    task.cancel(helperReceiverTeleportLoop2)
                    helperReceiverTeleportLoop2 = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

    })

    local receiverSlapAuraLoopMace = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("MaceReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverSlapAuraMace = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverSlapAuraMace = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverSlapAuraLoopMace then
                    task.cancel(receiverSlapAuraLoopMace)
                    receiverSlapAuraLoopMace = nil
                end

                receiverSlapAuraLoopMace = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverSlapAuraMace do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            generalHit:FireServer(targetPart, 93.05674743652344)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverSlapAuraLoopMace then
                    task.cancel(receiverSlapAuraLoopMace)
                    receiverSlapAuraLoopMace = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Mace mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperRagdollMace = false
    local helperRagdollLoopMace = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("MaceHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver and dies on ragdoll.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperRagdollMace = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperRagdollMace = false
                    return
                end

                if helperRagdollLoopMace then
                    task.cancel(helperRagdollLoopMace)
                    helperRagdollLoopMace = nil
                end

                helperRagdollLoopMace = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperRagdollMace do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")

                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperRagdollLoopMace then
                    task.cancel(helperRagdollLoopMace)
                    helperRagdollLoopMace = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

-- ENGINEER TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Engineer

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 500 Players with Engineer, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Engineer mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverSentry = false
    local receiverSentryLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("EngineerReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot and uses ability.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverSentry = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverSentry = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverSentryLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverSentryLoop)
                    receiverSentryLoop = nil
                end

                receiverSentryLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    local abilityTimer = 0

                    while autoReceiverSentry do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            abilityTimer = abilityTimer + 0.5
                            if abilityTimer >= 6 then
                                abilityTimer = 0
                                local sentry = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Sentry")
                                if sentry then
                                    sentry:FireServer()
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Sentry Ability Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverSentryLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverSentryLoop)
                    receiverSentryLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Engineer mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperSentry = false
    local helperSentryLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("EngineerHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver/Sentry's Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver or sentry's glove and dies on ragdoll.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperSentry = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperSentry = false
                    return
                end

                if helperSentryLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperSentryLoop)
                    helperSentryLoop = nil
                end

                helperSentryLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperSentry do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")

                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local turret = workspace:FindFirstChild("Turret")
                            if turret then
                                local hingePart = turret:FindFirstChild("HingePart")
                                if hingePart then
                                    local glove = hingePart:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                                    if glove then
                                        hrp.CFrame = glove.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperSentryLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperSentryLoop)

                end
            end
        end
    })

-- =================================================================================================
-- PHANTOM TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Phantom

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 500 Players with Phantom, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Phantom mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverPhantom = false
    local receiverPhantomLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("PhantomReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverPhantom = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverPhantom = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverPhantomLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverPhantomLoop)
                    receiverPhantomLoop = nil
                end

                receiverPhantomLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverPhantom do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local phantomDash = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PhantomDash")
                            if phantomDash then
                                local phantom = char and char:FindFirstChild("Phantom")
                                if phantom then
                                    phantomDash:InvokeServer(phantom)
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.01)

                            local phantomHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PhantomHit")
                            if phantomHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            phantomHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Phantom Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverPhantomLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverPhantomLoop)
                    receiverPhantomLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Phantom mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperReceiverTeleportPhantom = false
    local helperReceiverTeleportLoopPhantom = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("PhantomHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
        Description = "Teleports to the receiver position.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperReceiverTeleportPhantom = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperReceiverTeleportPhantom = false
                    return
                end

                if helperReceiverTeleportLoopPhantom then
                    task.cancel(helperReceiverTeleportLoopPhantom)
                    helperReceiverTeleportLoopPhantom = nil
                end

                helperReceiverTeleportLoopPhantom = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperReceiverTeleportPhantom do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    else
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto teleport to Receiver position enabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })

            else
                if helperReceiverTeleportLoopPhantom then
                    task.cancel(helperReceiverTeleportLoopPhantom)
                    helperReceiverTeleportLoopPhantom = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

-- WORMHOLE TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Wormhole

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 500 Players with Wormhole, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Wormhole mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverWormhole = false
    local receiverWormholeLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("WormholeReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura + Auto Teleport To Circle Portals",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, slaps, and teleports to portals.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverWormhole = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverWormhole = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverWormholeLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverWormholeLoop)
                    receiverWormholeLoop = nil
                end

                receiverWormholeLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    local portalTimer = 0

                    while autoReceiverWormhole do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local wormholePlace = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("WormholePlace")
                            if wormholePlace then
                                wormholePlace:FireServer()
                            end

                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local wormHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("WormHit")
                            if wormHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            wormHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            portalTimer = portalTimer + 0.5
                            if portalTimer >= 2 then
                                portalTimer = 0

                                local wormholes = workspace:FindFirstChild("Wormholes")
                                if wormholes then
                                    local one = wormholes:FindFirstChild("One")
                                    local two = wormholes:FindFirstChild("Two")

                                    if one and two and char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if portalTimer == 0 then
                                            hrp.CFrame = one.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                        else
                                            hrp.CFrame = two.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Wormhole Ability + Slap Aura + Portal Teleport Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverWormholeLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverWormholeLoop)
                    receiverWormholeLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Wormhole mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperReceiverWormhole = false
    local helperReceiverWormholeLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("WormholeHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
        Description = "Teleports to the receiver position.",

                    })
                    autoHelperReceiverWormhole = false
                    return
                end

                if helperReceiverWormholeLoop then

                    helperReceiverWormholeLoop = nil
                end

                helperReceiverWormholeLoop = task.spawn(function()

-- CHERRY TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Cherry

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3-4 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 500 Players with Cherry, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Cherry mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverCherry = false
    local receiverCherryLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("CherryReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura + Auto Use Ability + Auto Use Cherry's Clone Glove",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, slaps, uses ability, and uses clone glove.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverCherry = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverCherry = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverCherryLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverCherryLoop)
                    receiverCherryLoop = nil
                end

                receiverCherryLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    local cloneTimer = 0

                    while autoReceiverCherry do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                            if generalAbility then
                                generalAbility:FireServer()
                            end

                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            cloneTimer = cloneTimer + 0.5
                            if cloneTimer >= 0.5 then
                                cloneTimer = 0

                                local cherryStorage = workspace:FindFirstChild("cherry_storage")
                                if cherryStorage then
                                    for _, model in pairs(cherryStorage:GetChildren()) do
                                        if model:IsA("Model") and model.Name:lower():match("cherry") then
                                            local cloneRemote = model:FindFirstChild("clone_remote")
                                            if cloneRemote then
                                                pcall(function()
                                                    cloneRemote:FireServer()
                                                end)
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura + Ability + Cherry Clone Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverCherryLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverCherryLoop)
                    receiverCherryLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Cherry mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperCherry = false
    local helperCherryLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("CherryHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Teleport To Cherry's Clone Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver, clone glove, and dies on ragdoll.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperCherry = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperCherry = false
                    return
                end

                if helperCherryLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperCherryLoop)
                    helperCherryLoop = nil
                end

                helperCherryLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperCherry do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")

                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local cherryStorage = workspace:FindFirstChild("cherry_storage")
                            if cherryStorage then
                                for _, model in pairs(cherryStorage:GetChildren()) do
                                    if model:IsA("Model") and model.Name:lower():match("cherry") then
                                        local tool = model:FindFirstChild("Cherry")
                                        if tool then
                                            local glove = tool:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                                            if glove and glove:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                                hrp.CFrame = glove.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Cherry Clone Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperCherryLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperCherryLoop)
                    helperCherryLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end
