                    })
                    autoHelperReceiverSimple = false
                    return
                end

                if helperReceiverSimpleLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperReceiverSimpleLoop)
                    helperReceiverSimpleLoop = nil
                end

                helperReceiverSimpleLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperReceiverSimple do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    else
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto teleport to Receiver position enabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })

            else
                if helperReceiverSimpleLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperReceiverSimpleLoop)
                    helperReceiverSimpleLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- BONK TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.BONK

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 500 Players with BONK, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for BONK mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverBonk = false
    local receiverBonkLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("BONKReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverBonk = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverBonk = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverBonkLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverBonkLoop)
                    receiverBonkLoop = nil
                end

                receiverBonkLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverBonk do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local bonk = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("BONK")
                            if bonk then
                                bonk:FireServer(-0.2956634000001941)
                            end                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + BONK Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverBonkLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverBonkLoop)
                    receiverBonkLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for BONK mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperBonk = false
    local helperBonkLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("BONKHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver and dies on ragdoll.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperBonk = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperBonk = false
                    return
                end

                if helperBonkLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperBonkLoop)
                    helperBonkLoop = nil
                end

                helperBonkLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperBonk do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")

                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperBonkLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperBonkLoop)
                    helperBonkLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- CLOUD TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Cloud

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Hit 50 Players with Cloud"
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Cloud mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverLoopCloud = false
    local receiverLoopThreadCloud = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("CloudReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Cloud Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Auto Teleport To Cloud + Auto Teleport 10 Studs High With Cloud + Auto Jump From Cloud + Auto Use Slap Aura",
        Description = "Full Cloud mastery automation.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverLoopCloud = Value

            if Value then
                if receiverLoopThreadCloud then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadCloud)
                    receiverLoopThreadCloud = nil
                end

                receiverLoopThreadCloud = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverLoopCloud do
                        pcall(function()
                            local CloudSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("CloudSafespot")
                            if CloudSafespot then
                                local base = CloudSafespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                    if char then
                                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if hrp then
                                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(base.Position + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0))
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local cloudAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("CloudAbility")
                            if cloudAbility then
                                cloudAbility:FireServer()
                            end
                            task.wait(0.3)

                            local playerName = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name
                            local cloud = workspace:FindFirstChild(playerName .. "_Cloud")
                            if cloud then
                                local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                if char then
                                    local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if hrp then
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(cloud.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                            task.wait(0.3)

                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    hrp.CFrame = hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            end
                            task.wait(0.2)

                            if char then
                                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                                if humanoid then
                                    humanoid.Jump = true
                                end
                            end
                            task.wait(1)

                            local cloudHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("CloudHit")
                            if cloudHit then
                                local startTime = tick()
                                while autoReceiverLoopCloud and (tick() - startTime) < 2 do
                                    pcall(function()
                                        for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                            if player.Character then
                                                local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                                if targetPart then
                                                    cloudHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                                end
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end)
                                    task.wait(0.5)
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(2)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Receiver Loop",
                    Content = "Auto Receiver Loop Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverLoopThreadCloud then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadCloud)
                    receiverLoopThreadCloud = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Cloud mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverSafespotCloud = false
    local receiverSafespotLoopCloud = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("CloudHelperTeleport", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
        Description = "Teleports to the cloud safespot.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverSafespotCloud = Value

            if Value then
                local CloudSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("CloudSafespot")
                if not CloudSafespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Cloud Safespot not found! Create Cloud Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverSafespotCloud = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverSafespotLoopCloud then
                    task.cancel(receiverSafespotLoopCloud)
                    receiverSafespotLoopCloud = nil
                end

                receiverSafespotLoopCloud = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverSafespotCloud do
                        pcall(function()
                            local CloudSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("CloudSafespot")
                            if CloudSafespot then
                                local base = CloudSafespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                    if char then
                                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if hrp then
                                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(base.Position + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0))
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Teleport",
                    Content = "Auto teleport to Cloud Safespot enabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })

            else
                if receiverSafespotLoopCloud then
                    task.cancel(receiverSafespotLoopCloud)
                    receiverSafespotLoopCloud = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "2 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Hit 200 Players with Cloud"
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Cloud Safespot",
        Description = "Teleports you to the cloud safespot.",
        Callback = function()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local character = player.Character

            local hasCloudGlove = player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Cloud"
            local hasEntered = character and character:FindFirstChild("entered")
            local hasCloudSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("CloudSafespot")

            if not hasCloudGlove or not hasEntered or not hasCloudSafespot then
                local errorMsg = ""
                if not hasCloudGlove then
                    errorMsg = "Equip Cloud Glove"
                elseif not hasEntered then
                    errorMsg = "Enter Arena First"
                elseif not hasCloudSafespot then
                    errorMsg = "Create Cloud Safespot First"
                end

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return
            end

            local Cloudsafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("CloudSafespot")
            if Cloudsafespot then
                local base = Cloudsafespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                if base then
                    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if hrp then
                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)

                        Fluent:Notify({
                            Title = "Teleported",
                            Content = "Teleported to Safespot!",
                            Duration = 2
                        })
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "3 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Fly 10K Studs with Cloud"
    })

    local SetSpeedCloud = 50
    Tab:AddSlider("CloudSpeed", {
        Title = "Set Speed Cloud",
        Description = "Adjusts the cloud speed multiplier.",
        Min = 0.1,
        Max = 100,
        Default = 50,
        Rounding = 0.1,
        Callback = function(Value)
            SetSpeedCloud = Value
        end
    })

    local CloudSpeed = false
    Tab:AddToggle("CloudSpeedToggle", {
        Title = "Auto Set Cloud Speed",
        Description = "Automatically sets the cloud speed.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            CloudSpeed = Value

            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Cloud" then
                while CloudSpeed and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Cloud" do
                    for i, v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                        if v.Name:match(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name) and v:FindFirstChild("BodyVelocity") then
                            v.BodyVelocity.Velocity = v.BodyVelocity.Velocity * SetSpeedCloud
                        end
                    end
                    task.wait(0.10)
                end
            elseif CloudSpeed == true then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Cloud",
                    Duration = 5
                })
                wait(0.05)
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "4 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Hit 500 Players with Cloud"
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Cloud mastery."
    })

    local PlayersList = {}

    local function RefreshPlayersList()
        PlayersList = {}
        for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                table.insert(PlayersList, player.Name)
            end
        end
        return PlayersList
    end

    local SelectedPlayer = nil
    local Dropdown = Tab:AddDropdown("CloudTargetPlayer", {
        Title = "Select Player",
        Description = "Select a player to target.",
        Values = RefreshPlayersList(),
        Multi = false,
        Default = 1,
        Callback = function(Value)
            SelectedPlayer = Value
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Refresh Players List",
        Description = "Refreshes the player list.",
        Callback = function()
            Dropdown:SetValues(RefreshPlayersList(), 1)
        end
    })

    local autoCloudLoop = false
    local cloudLoopThread = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("CloudJumpHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Choosed Player's Cloud + Auto Jump From Cloud",
        Description = "Teleports to selected player's cloud and jumps.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoCloudLoop = Value

            if Value then
                if not SelectedPlayer or SelectedPlayer == "" then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Please select a player first!",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoCloudLoop = false
                    return
                end

                local playerExists = false
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player.Name == SelectedPlayer then
                        playerExists = true
                        break
                    end
                end

                if not playerExists then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Selected player no longer exists!",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoCloudLoop = false
                    return
                end

                if cloudLoopThread then
                    task.cancel(cloudLoopThread)
                    cloudLoopThread = nil
                end

                cloudLoopThread = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoCloudLoop do
                        local playerExists = false
                        for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                            if player.Name == SelectedPlayer then
                                playerExists = true
                                break
                            end
                        end

                        if not playerExists then
                            Fluent:Notify({
                                Title = "Warning",
                                Content = "Selected player left the game!",
                                Duration = 3
                            })
                            autoCloudLoop = false
                            break
                        end

                        pcall(function()
                            local cloudName = SelectedPlayer .. "_Cloud"
                            local cloud = Workspace:FindFirstChild(cloudName)

                            if cloud then
                                local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                                if char then
                                    local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if hrp then
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(cloud.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                                        task.wait(0.1)

                                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                                        if humanoid then
                                            humanoid.Jump = true
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            else
                                for _, obj in pairs(Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                    if obj:IsA("BasePart") and string.find(obj.Name, SelectedPlayer) and string.find(obj.Name, "Cloud") then
                                        local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                                        if char then
                                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                            if hrp then
                                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(obj.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                                                task.wait(0.1)

                                                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                                                if humanoid then
                                                    humanoid.Jump = true
                                                end
                                            end
                                        end
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)

                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Cloud Helper",
                    Content = "Auto teleport to " .. SelectedPlayer .. "'s cloud + jump enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if cloudLoopThread then
                    task.cancel(cloudLoopThread)
                    cloudLoopThread = nil
                end

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Cloud Helper",
                    Content = "Auto teleport + jump disabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })
end

-- REDACTED TAB

do
    local Tab = Tabs.REDACTED

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with [REDACTED], etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for [REDACTED] mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverWell = false
    local receiverWellLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("REDACTEDReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot and uses ability.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverWell = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverWell = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverWellLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverWellLoop)
                    receiverWellLoop = nil
                end

                receiverWellLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    local abilityTimer = 0

                    while autoReceiverWell do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            abilityTimer = abilityTimer + 0.5
                            if abilityTimer >= 5 then
                                abilityTimer = 0
                                local well = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Well")
                                if well then
                                    well:FireServer()
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Well Ability Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverWellLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverWellLoop)
                    receiverWellLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for [REDACTED] mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperWell = false
    local helperWellLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("REDACTEDHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Teleport To Pocket Dimension Portal",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver and portal.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperWell = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperWell = false
                    return
                end

                if helperWellLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperWellLoop)
                    helperWellLoop = nil
                end

                helperWellLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperWell do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")

                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local wellModel = workspace:FindFirstChild("WellModel")
                            if wellModel then
                                local part = wellModel:FindFirstChild("Part")
                                if part and part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    hrp.CFrame = part.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Pocket Dimension Portal Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperWellLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperWellLoop)
                    helperWellLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

-- BUS TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.bus

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with Bus, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Bus mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverBus = false
    local receiverBusLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("BusReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverBus = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverBus = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverBusLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverBusLoop)
                    receiverBusLoop = nil
                end

                receiverBusLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    local abilityTimer = 0

                    while autoReceiverBus do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            abilityTimer = abilityTimer + 0.5
                            if abilityTimer >= 5.5 then
                                abilityTimer = 0
                                local busmoment = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("busmoment")
                                if busmoment then
                                    busmoment:FireServer()
                                end
                            end

                            local hitbus = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("hitbus")
                            if hitbus then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            hitbus:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Bus Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverBusLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverBusLoop)
                    receiverBusLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Bus mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperBus = false
    local helperBusLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("BusHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Teleport To Bus",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver and then to the bus.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperBus = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperBus = false
                    return
                end

                if helperBusLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperBusLoop)
                    helperBusLoop = nil
                end

                helperBusLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperBus do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")

                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local busModel = workspace:FindFirstChild("BusModel")
                            if busModel and busModel:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                hrp.CFrame = busModel.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                            else
                                for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                    if obj:IsA("MeshPart") and obj.Name == "BusModel" then
                                        hrp.CFrame = obj.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Bus Teleport Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperBusLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperBusLoop)
                    helperBusLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "2 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Use Bus 1000 Times"
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Spawn Bus (Normal)",
        Description = "Spawns the bus normally.",
        Callback = function()
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Bus" then
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").busmoment:FireServer()
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Bus",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Spawn Bus (Fast + Kicks)",
        Description = "Spawns the bus rapidly.",
        Callback = function()
            while true do
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").busmoment:FireServer()
                wait()
            end
        end
    })
end

    local Tab = Tabs.Phase

    })

        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Phase mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverPhase = false
    local receiverPhaseLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("PhaseReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverPhase = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverPhase = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverPhaseLoop then
                    task.cancel(receiverPhaseLoop)
                    receiverPhaseLoop = nil
                end

                receiverPhaseLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    local abilityTimer = 0

                    while autoReceiverPhase do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            abilityTimer = abilityTimer + 0.5
                            if abilityTimer >= 14 then
                                abilityTimer = 0
                                local phaseA = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PhaseA")
                                if phaseA then
                                    phaseA:FireServer()
                                end
                            end

                            local phaseH = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PhaseH")
