                    receiverPhaseLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Phase mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperReceiverPhase = false
    local helperReceiverPhaseLoop = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("PhaseHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
        Description = "Teleports to the receiver position.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperReceiverPhase = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperReceiverPhase = false
                    return
                end

                if helperReceiverPhaseLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperReceiverPhaseLoop)
                    helperReceiverPhaseLoop = nil
                end

                helperReceiverPhaseLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperReceiverPhase do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    else
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Auto teleport to Receiver position enabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })

            else
                if helperReceiverPhaseLoop then
                    task.cancel(helperReceiverPhaseLoop)
                    helperReceiverPhaseLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "2 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Hit 100 Players with Phase"
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Auto Ability + Teleport To All Islands (Takes 112 Seconds)",
        Description = "Automatically uses Phase ability and teleports to all islands.",
        Callback = function()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

            if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Phase" and player.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                local function phaseTo(position)
                    player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(122, 255, 3)
                    task.wait(0.1)
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").PhaseA:FireServer()
                    task.wait(0.1)
                    player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(position)
                    task.wait(14)
                end

                phaseTo(Vector3.new(236, -16, -6))
                phaseTo(Vector3.new())
                phaseTo(Vector3.new(4, -5, -223))
                phaseTo(Vector3.new(-216, -5, -6))
                phaseTo(Vector3.new(-401, 51, -16))
                phaseTo(Vector3.new(256, 34, 194))
                phaseTo(Vector3.new(4, -5, 215))
                phaseTo(Vector3.new(-125, -5, 122))
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Phase Glove/Use In Arena",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- BOMB TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Bomb

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 500 Players with Bomb, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddToggle("BombAuto", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and dies on ragdoll.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            if Value then
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

                if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value ~= "Bomb" then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Equip Bomb Glove",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    return false
                end

                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Create Safespot first!",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    return false
                end

                getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop = true

                task.spawn(function()
                    while getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")

                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end
                            task.wait(1)

                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(1)
                                return
                            end

                            local bombThrow = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("BombThrow")
                            if bombThrow then
                                bombThrow:FireServer("Ebutton")
                            end
                            task.wait(1)

                            local bombFound = false
                            for i = 1, 30 do
                                if not getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop then break end

                                for _, v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                    if v.Name and string.find(v.Name, "_bømb") then
                                        hrp.CFrame = v.CFrame
                                        bombFound = true
                                        break
                                    end
                                end

                                if bombFound then
                                    break
                                else
                                    task.wait(1)
                                end
                            end

                            ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(1)
                                return
                            end

                            if humanoid then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(1)
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Bomb Tasks",
                    Content = "Started! Teleporting to Safespot + Using Bomb",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop = false
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Use Bomb"
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Throw Bomb/Explode Bomb",
        Description = "Throws and explodes the bomb.",
        Callback = function()
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Bomb" then
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").BombThrow:FireServer("Ebutton")
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Bomb",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- BUBBLE TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Bubble

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3-4 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with Bubble, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Bubble mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverBubble = false
    local receiverLoopThreadBubble = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("BubbleReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverBubble = Value

            if Value then
                if receiverLoopThreadBubble then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadBubble)
                    receiverLoopThreadBubble = nil
                end

                receiverLoopThreadBubble = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverBubble do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if not char then return end
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not hrp then return end

                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local bubbleThrow = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("BubbleThrow")
                            if bubbleThrow then
                                bubbleThrow:FireServer()
                            end

                            local bubbleHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("BubbleHit")
                            if bubbleHit then
                                local startTime = tick()
                                while autoReceiverBubble and (tick() - startTime) < 6 do
                                    pcall(function()
                                        for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                            if player.Character then
                                                local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                                if targetPart then
                                                    bubbleHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                                end
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end)
                                    task.wait(0.5)
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(1)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Receiver Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverLoopThreadBubble then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadBubble)
                    receiverLoopThreadBubble = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Bubble mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperBubble = false
    local helperLoopThreadBubble = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("BubbleHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Enter Arena + Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Teleport To Bubble Object + Auto Die When Bubble Object Dissapears",
        Description = "Enters arena, teleports to receiver, bubble object, and dies when it disappears.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperBubble = Value

            if Value then
                if helperLoopThreadBubble then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopThreadBubble)
                    helperLoopThreadBubble = nil
                end

                helperLoopThreadBubble = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperBubble do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if not char then return end
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not hrp then return end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(1)
                            end
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            task.wait(0.3)

                            local bubbleFound = false
                            local bubblePart = nil

                            for _, obj in pairs(Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                if obj:IsA("Model") and obj.Name == "BubbleObject" then
                                    for _, part in pairs(obj:GetDescendants()) do
                                        if part:IsA("BasePart") or part:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                            bubblePart = part
                                            bubbleFound = true
                                            break
                                        end
                                    end
                                elseif obj:IsA("BasePart") or obj:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                    if obj.Name == "BubbleObject" or string.find(obj.Name, "Bubble") then
                                        bubblePart = obj
                                        bubbleFound = true
                                    end
                                end

                                if bubbleFound then break end
                            end

                            if bubbleFound and bubblePart then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(bubblePart.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                                task.wait(0.3)
                            else
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local bubbleStillExists = false
                            for _, obj in pairs(Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                if obj:IsA("Model") and obj.Name == "BubbleObject" then
                                    bubbleStillExists = true
                                    break
                                elseif obj:IsA("BasePart") or obj:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                    if obj.Name == "BubbleObject" or string.find(obj.Name, "Bubble") then
                                        bubbleStillExists = true
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            if not bubbleStillExists then
                                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                                if humanoid then
                                    humanoid.Health = 0
                                end
                                task.wait(1)
                            else
                                task.wait(1)
                            end
                        end)

                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Helper Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperLoopThreadBubble then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopThreadBubble)
                    helperLoopThreadBubble = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- SHARD TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Shard

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3-4-5 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 500 Players with Shard, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Shard mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverShard = false
    local receiverLoopThreadShard = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("ShardReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura + Auto Use Ability",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, slaps, and uses ability.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverShard = Value

            if Value then
                if receiverLoopThreadShard then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadShard)
                    receiverLoopThreadShard = nil
                end

                receiverLoopThreadShard = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverShard do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if not char then return end
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not hrp then return end

                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10225, -42, 9986)
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local shardsEvent = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Events")
                            if shardsEvent then
                                local shards = shardsEvent:FindFirstChild("Shards")
                                if shards then
                                    shards:FireServer()
                                end
                            end

                            local shardHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("ShardHIT")
                            if shardHit then
                                local startTime = tick()
                                while autoReceiverShard and (tick() - startTime) < 6 do
                                    pcall(function()
                                        for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                            if player.Character then
                                                local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                    player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                                if targetPart then
                                                    shardHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                                end
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end)
                                    task.wait(0.5)
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(1)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Receiver Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverLoopThreadShard then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadShard)
                    receiverLoopThreadShard = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Shard mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperShard = false
    local helperLoopThreadShard = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("ShardHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Teleport To Shards Object",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver and shard object.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperShard = Value

            if Value then
                if helperLoopThreadShard then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopThreadShard)
                    helperLoopThreadShard = nil
                end

                helperLoopThreadShard = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperShard do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if not char then return end
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not hrp then return end

                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local shotShard = workspace:FindFirstChild("ShotShard")
                            if shotShard then
                                if shotShard:IsA("Model") then
                                    local targetPart = shotShard:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or
                                        shotShard:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                        shotShard:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                        shotShard:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPart.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                                    end
                                elseif shotShard:IsA("BasePart") or shotShard:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(shotShard.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                                end
                            else
                                local shardFound = false
                                for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                    if obj:IsA("BasePart") and string.find(obj.Name, "Shard") then
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(obj.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                                        shardFound = true
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Helper Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperLoopThreadShard then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopThreadShard)
                    helperLoopThreadShard = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- MOON TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Moon

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with Moon, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Moon mastery."
    })

    local moonToggle = false

    Tab:AddToggle("MoonReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Ragdoll + Auto Equip/Unequip Glove + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, ragdolls, equips/unequips glove, and slaps.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            moonToggle = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    return false
                end

                task.spawn(function()
                    while moonToggle do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                local moonRagdollLoop = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                    if not moonToggle then return end
                    pcall(function()
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                            game.ReplicatedStorage.SelfKnockback:FireServer({
                                ["Force"] = 0,
                                ["Direction"] = Vector3.new(0, 0.01, 0)
                            })
                        end
                    end)
                end)

                local moonGloveLoop = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                    if not moonToggle then return end
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                        local character = player.Character

                        if backpack and character then
                            local moonTool = backpack:FindFirstChild("Moon") or character:FindFirstChild("Moon")
                            if moonTool then
                                local currentlyEquipped = character:FindFirstChild("Moon")
                                if currentlyEquipped then
                                    moonTool.Parent = backpack
                                else
                                    moonTool.Parent = character
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end)

                task.spawn(function()
                    while moonToggle do
                        pcall(function()
                            local celestialHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("CelestialHit")
                            if celestialHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            celestialHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Moon",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Ragdoll + Equip/Unequip + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            else
                moonToggle = false
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Moon mastery."
    })

    Tab:AddToggle("MoonHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
        Description = "Teleports to the receiver position.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            if Value then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while Value do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    else
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    })
end

    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Place Tycoon To Safe Spot",
        Description = "Places a tycoon in a safe spot.",
        Callback = function()
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Tycoon" then
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

                local args = {
                    [1] = CFrame.new(17893.552734375, -26.257728576660156, -3535.35888671875,

                        0.9999628067016602, -1.1323045834288337e-09, 0.00862560048699379)
                }

                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("GeneralAbility"):FireServer(unpack(args))
                task.wait(1)

                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Success",
                    Content = "Tycoon placed at safe spot!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Tycoon Glove",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- MOAI TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Moai

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with 🗿, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for 🗿 mastery."
    })

    local moaiToggle = false

    Tab:AddToggle("MoaiReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            moaiToggle = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    return false
                end

                task.spawn(function()
                    while moaiToggle do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                            if generalAbility then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        local args = {
                                            [1] = base.CFrame
                                        }
                                        generalAbility:FireServer(unpack(args))
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(14)

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "🗿",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for 🗿 mastery."
    })

    Tab:AddToggle("MoaiHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver and dies on ragdoll.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            if Value then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while Value do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then return end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    })
end

    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Obby Slap Aura",
        Description = "Slaps all players continuously for Obby mastery.",
        Callback = function()
            task.spawn(function()
                local players = game:GetService("Players")
                local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
                local localPlayer = players.LocalPlayer

                while true do
                    pcall(function()
                        for _, player in ipairs(players:GetPlayers()) do
                            if player ~= localPlayer then
                                local character = player.Character
                                if character then
                                    local leftArm = character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm")
                                    if leftArm then
                                        replicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(leftArm)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- VOODOO TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Voodoo

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with Voodoo, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Voodoo mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverVoodoo = false
    local receiverLoopThreadVoodoo = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("VoodooReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura Player/Voodoo Doll",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and slaps players/dolls.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverVoodoo = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    print("⚠️ No Safespot found, using hardcoded position")
                end

                if receiverLoopThreadVoodoo then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadVoodoo)
                    receiverLoopThreadVoodoo = nil
                end

                receiverLoopThreadVoodoo = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverVoodoo do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                else
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                            if generalAbility then
                                generalAbility:FireServer()
                            end

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local startTime = tick()
                                while autoReceiverVoodoo and (tick() - startTime) < 4 do
                                    pcall(function()
                                        for _, targetPlayer in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                            if targetPlayer.Character then
                                                local targetParts = {
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm"),
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm"),
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head"),
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso"),
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"),
                                                    targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("DOLLPART")
                                                }

                                                for _, part in pairs(targetParts) do
                                                    if part then
                                                        generalHit:FireServer(part)
                                                    end
                                                end

                                                for _, child in pairs(targetPlayer.Character:GetChildren()) do
                                                    if child.Name == "DOLLPART" and child:IsA("BasePart") then
                                                        generalHit:FireServer(child)
                                                    end
                                                end
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end)
                                    task.wait(0.5)
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Receiver Enabled! (Safespot + Ability + Slap Aura)",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverLoopThreadVoodoo then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadVoodoo)
                    receiverLoopThreadVoodoo = nil
                end

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Receiver Disabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Voodoo mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperVoodoo = false
    local helperLoopThreadVoodoo = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("VoodooHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver and dies on ragdoll.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperVoodoo = Value

            if Value then
                if helperLoopThreadVoodoo then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopThreadVoodoo)
                    helperLoopThreadVoodoo = nil
                end

                helperLoopThreadVoodoo = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperVoodoo do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(1)
                                return
                            end

                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Helper Enabled! (Receiver + Die On Ragdoll)",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperLoopThreadVoodoo then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopThreadVoodoo)
                    helperLoopThreadVoodoo = nil
                end

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Helper Disabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })
end

-- ROB TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.rob

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with rob, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Get Bob Glove"
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Create Null Portal (Need Bob And Rob Gloves)",
        Description = "Creates a null portal using Bob and Rob gloves.",
        Callback = function()
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local hrp = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

            if not hrp then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Character not found!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return
            end

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new()
            task.wait(0.5)

            local robClick = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby") and workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild("rob") and workspace.Lobby.rob:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector")
            if robClick then
                fireclickdetector(robClick)
            end
            task.wait(0.5)

            local robRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("rob")
            if robRemote then
                robRemote:FireServer()
            end
            task.wait(0.5)

            local bobClick = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby") and workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild("bob") and workspace.Lobby.bob:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector")
            if bobClick then
                fireclickdetector(bobClick)
            end
            task.wait(0.5)

            local bobRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("bob")
            if bobRemote then
                bobRemote:FireServer()
            end

            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Done",
                Content = "Null Portal sequence completed!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "2 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Kill 100 Players with rob"
    })

    local Walkspeed = 20
    local KeepWalkspeed = false

    Tab:AddSlider("RobWalkspeed", {
        Title = "WalkSpeed",
        Description = "Sets your walk speed.",
        Min = 20,
        Max = 1000,
        Default = 20,
        Rounding = 1,
        Callback = function(Value)
            Walkspeed = Value
            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if char then
                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                if humanoid then
                    humanoid.WalkSpeed = Value
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddInput("RobWalkspeedInput", {
        Title = "WalkSpeed",
        Description = "Sets your walk speed via input.",
        Default = "20",
        Placeholder = "20",
        Numeric = true,
        Finished = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            local num = tonumber(Value)
            if num then
                Walkspeed = num
                local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                if char then
                    local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                    if humanoid then
                        humanoid.WalkSpeed = num
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddToggle("RobWalkspeedAuto", {
        Title = "Walkspeed Set Auto",
        Description = "Automatically sets walk speed.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            KeepWalkspeed = Value
            if Value then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while KeepWalkspeed do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                                if humanoid and humanoid.WalkSpeed ~= Walkspeed then
                                    humanoid.WalkSpeed = Walkspeed
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "3 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Absorb 100 Players with rob"
    })

    local AutoAbsorb = false

    Tab:AddToggle("RobAbsorb", {
        Title = "Auto Absorb People",
        Description = "Automatically absorbs people with rob glove.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            AutoAbsorb = Value
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

            if AutoAbsorb then
                if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value:lower() == "rob" then
                    task.spawn(function()
                        while AutoAbsorb do
                            pcall(function()
                                local players = game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()
                                local target = nil
                                local attempts = 0

                                while not target and attempts < 20 do
                                    attempts = attempts + 1
                                    local randomPlayer = players[math.random(1, #players)]
                                    if randomPlayer ~= player and randomPlayer.Character and randomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                        target = randomPlayer
                                    end
                                end

                                if target then
                                    local targetHRP = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    local playerHRP = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

                                    if targetHRP and playerHRP then
                                        playerHRP.CFrame = targetHRP.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 0, 2)
                                    end

                                    local ability = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Ability")
                                    if ability then
                                        ability:FireServer()
                                    end
                                end
                            end)
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                    end)
                else
                    AutoAbsorb = false
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Equip Rob Glove",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end
    })

    local autoRobLoop = false

    Tab:AddToggle("RobTransformation", {
        Title = "Auto Rob Transformation",
        Description = "Automatically transforms into rob.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoRobLoop = Value

            if Value then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while autoRobLoop do
                        pcall(function()
                            local robObject = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby")
                            if robObject then
                                robObject = robObject:FindFirstChild("rob")
                                if robObject and robObject:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                                    fireclickdetector(robObject.ClickDetector)
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local robRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("rob")
                            if robRemote then
                                robRemote:FireServer()
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(17)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- FIREWORK TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Firework

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with Firework, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Firework mastery."
    })

    local autoReceiverFirework = false
    local receiverLoopFirework = nil
    local slapAuraConnectionFirework = nil
    local abilityConnectionFirework = nil
    local fireworkConnectionFirework = nil
    local jumpTimerFirework = 0
    local abilityTimerFirework = 0
    local slapTimerFirework = 0
    local fireworkTimerFirework = 0

    Tab:AddToggle("FireworkReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Receiver (Safespot + Ability + Firework + Jump + Slap Aura)",
        Description = "Full Firework mastery automation.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverFirework = Value

            if Value then
                jumpTimerFirework = 0
                abilityTimerFirework = 0
                slapTimerFirework = 0
                fireworkTimerFirework = 0

                if receiverLoopFirework then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopFirework)
                    receiverLoopFirework = nil
                end

                receiverLoopFirework = task.spawn(function()
                    local jumpTimer = 0

                    while autoReceiverFirework do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character
                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not hrp then return end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base and base:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            end

                            jumpTimer = jumpTimer + 0.01
                            if jumpTimer >= 4 then
                                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                if humanoid then
                                    humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
                                end
                                jumpTimer = 0
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.01)
                    end
                end)

                if fireworkConnectionFirework then
                    fireworkConnectionFirework:Disconnect()
                    fireworkConnectionFirework = nil
                end

                fireworkConnectionFirework = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
                    if not autoReceiverFirework then
                        fireworkConnectionFirework:Disconnect()
                        fireworkConnectionFirework = nil
                        return
                    end

                    fireworkTimerFirework = fireworkTimerFirework + deltaTime
                    if fireworkTimerFirework >= 1 then
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character
                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not hrp then return end

                            local playerName = player.Name
                            local fireworkPart = workspace:FindFirstChild("Firework_" .. playerName)
                            if fireworkPart and fireworkPart:IsA("BasePart") then
                                hrp.CFrame = fireworkPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)
                            end
                        end)
                        fireworkTimerFirework = 0
                    end
                end)

                if abilityConnectionFirework then
                    abilityConnectionFirework:Disconnect()
                    abilityConnectionFirework = nil
                end

                abilityConnectionFirework = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
                    if not autoReceiverFirework then
                        abilityConnectionFirework:Disconnect()
                        abilityConnectionFirework = nil
                        return
                    end

                    abilityTimerFirework = abilityTimerFirework + deltaTime
                    if abilityTimerFirework >= 3 then
                        pcall(function()
                            local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                            if generalAbility then
                                generalAbility:FireServer()
                            end
                        end)
                        abilityTimerFirework = 0
                    end
                end)

                if slapAuraConnectionFirework then
                    slapAuraConnectionFirework:Disconnect()
                    slapAuraConnectionFirework = nil
                end

                slapAuraConnectionFirework = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
                    if not autoReceiverFirework then
                        slapAuraConnectionFirework:Disconnect()
                        slapAuraConnectionFirework = nil
                        return
                    end

                    slapTimerFirework = slapTimerFirework + deltaTime
                    if slapTimerFirework >= 3 then
                        pcall(function()
                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if not generalHit then return end

                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                        player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                        player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                        player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                        player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        slapTimerFirework = 0
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Receiver",
                    Content = "Enabled! Safespot at 0.01s, Firework at 1s, others at 3s.",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverLoopFirework then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopFirework)
                    receiverLoopFirework = nil
                end

                if fireworkConnectionFirework then
                    fireworkConnectionFirework:Disconnect()
                    fireworkConnectionFirework = nil
                end

                if abilityConnectionFirework then
                    abilityConnectionFirework:Disconnect()
                    abilityConnectionFirework = nil
                end

                if slapAuraConnectionFirework then
                    slapAuraConnectionFirework:Disconnect()
                    slapAuraConnectionFirework = nil
                end

                jumpTimerFirework = 0
                abilityTimerFirework = 0
                slapTimerFirework = 0
                fireworkTimerFirework = 0
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Firework mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperFirework = false
    local helperLoopFirework = nil
    local helperJumpTimerFirework = 0

    Tab:AddToggle("FireworkHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Helper (Safespot + Firework + Jump + Die on Ragdoll + Auto Re-enter)",
        Description = "Helper automation for Firework mastery.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperFirework = Value

            if Value then
                helperJumpTimerFirework = 0

                if helperLoopFirework then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopFirework)
                    helperLoopFirework = nil
                end

                helperLoopFirework = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperFirework do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character
                            if not char then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not hrp then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                                return
                            end

                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)

                            for _, part in ipairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                if part:IsA("BasePart") and string.find(part.Name, "Firework") then
                                    hrp.CFrame = part.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)
                                    break
                                end
                            end

                            helperJumpTimerFirework = helperJumpTimerFirework + 0.5
                            if helperJumpTimerFirework >= 4 then
                                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                if humanoid then
                                    humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
                                end
                                helperJumpTimerFirework = 0
                            end

                            local entered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")

                            if entered == nil then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            else
                                local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                                if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                    local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                    if humanoid then
                                        humanoid.Health = 0
                                        task.wait(2)

                                        local newChar = player.Character
                                        if newChar then
                                            local newHrp = newChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                            if newHrp then
                                                newHrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                                task.wait(0.5)
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Auto Helper",
                    Content = "Enabled! Teleporting to Safespot, Firework, Jumping & monitoring ragdoll.",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperLoopFirework then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopFirework)
                    helperLoopFirework = nil
                end

                helperJumpTimerFirework = 0
            end
        end
    })
end
