-- GLOVEL TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Glovel

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2-3 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with Glovel, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Glovel mastery."
    })

    local glovelToggle = false

    Tab:AddToggle("GlovelReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            glovelToggle = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    return false
                end

                task.spawn(function()
                    while glovelToggle do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local glovelFunc = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GlovelFunc")
                            if glovelFunc then
                                glovelFunc:InvokeServer()
                            end

                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local head = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                                        if head then
                                            generalHit:FireServer(head, true)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Glovel",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Glovel mastery."
    })

    Tab:AddToggle("GlovelHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
        Description = "Teleports to the receiver position.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            if Value then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while Value do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    else
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    })
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- RUN TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.Run

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2 Quests",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with Run, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Closest Player",
        Description = "Teleports to the closest player.",
        Callback = function()
            local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
            local localChar = LocalPlayer.Character
            local localHRP = localChar and localChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

            if not localHRP then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Your character not found!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
                return
            end

            local closestPlayer = nil
            local closestDistance = math.huge
            local closestPos = nil

            for _, player in ipairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local character = player.Character
                    local hrp = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if hrp then
                        local distance = (hrp.Position - localHRP.Position).Magnitude
                        if distance < closestDistance then
                            closestDistance = distance
                            closestPlayer = player
                            closestPos = hrp.Position
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            if closestPlayer and closestPos then
                localHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(closestPos)
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Teleported",
                    Content = "Teleported to " .. closestPlayer.Name .. " (" .. math.floor(closestDistance) .. " studs away)",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "No other players found!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })

    local positionValue = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
    local secondsValue = 7

    local positionInput = Tab:AddInput("RunPosition", {
        Title = "Put Position (x, y, z)",
        Description = "Enter coordinates separated by commas.",
        Default = "0, 0, 0",
        Placeholder = "0, 0, 0",
        Numeric = false,
        Finished = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            local parts = {}
            for part in string.gmatch(Value, "([^,]+)") do
                table.insert(parts, tonumber(part))
            end

            if #parts >= 3 and parts[1] and parts[2] and parts[3] then
                positionValue = Vector3.new(parts[1], parts[2], parts[3])
            else
                positionValue = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
            end
        end
    })

    local secondsInput = Tab:AddInput("RunDelay", {
        Title = "Repeat Ability Seconds Delay",
        Description = "Delay between ability uses.",
        Default = "7",
        Placeholder = "7",
        Numeric = true,
        Finished = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            local num = tonumber(Value)
            if num and num > 0 then
                secondsValue = num
            else
                secondsValue = 7
            end
        end
    })

    local autoRunEnabled = false

    Tab:AddToggle("RunAuto", {
        Title = "Auto Use Run Ability",
        Description = "Automatically uses the Run ability.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoRunEnabled = Value

            if Value then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while autoRunEnabled do
                        pcall(function()
                            local args = {
                                [1] = positionValue
                            }
                            local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                            if generalAbility then
                                generalAbility:FireServer(unpack(args))
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(secondsValue)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    })
end

                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                            if generalAbility then
                                generalAbility:FireServer(0.012500000651925802)
                            end

                            task.wait(4)

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do

            if Value then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while Value do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then return end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    })

-- =================================================================================================
-- CAR KEYS TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.CarKeys

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1 Quest",
        Content = "Quest: Upgrade Car Keys 100 Times"
    })

    local carKeysToggle = false
    local upgradeLoop = nil

    local attributeFrames = {
        "UtilityAttributeFrame",
        "ArmorAttributeFrame",
        "ReverseAttributeFrame",
        "SteerAngleAttributeFrame",
        "AccelerationAttributeFrame",
        "MaxSpeedAttributeFrame",
        "KnockbackAttributeFrame"
    }

    Tab:AddToggle("CarKeysUpgrade", {
        Title = "Auto Upgrade All Stats",
        Description = "Automatically upgrades all car stats.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            carKeysToggle = Value
            if carKeysToggle then
                upgradeLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while carKeysToggle do
                        for _, attr in ipairs(attributeFrames) do
                            local args = { attr }
                            local carKeysUpgrade = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("CarKeysUpgrade")
                            if carKeysUpgrade then
                                carKeysUpgrade:FireServer(unpack(args))
                            end
                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
            else
                if upgradeLoop then
                    task.cancel(upgradeLoop)
                    upgradeLoop = nil
                end
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "2-3 Quests",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with Car Keys, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Car Keys mastery."
    })

    local SelectedPlayer = nil
    local PlayersList = {}

    local function RefreshPlayersList()
        PlayersList = {}
        for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                table.insert(PlayersList, player.Name)
            end
        end
        return PlayersList
    end

    local Dropdown = Tab:AddDropdown("CarKeysTargetPlayer", {
        Title = "Select Player",
        Description = "Select a player to target.",
        Values = RefreshPlayersList(),
        Multi = false,
        Default = 1,
        Callback = function(Value)
            SelectedPlayer = Value
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Refresh Players List",
        Description = "Refreshes the player list.",
        Callback = function()
            Dropdown:SetValues(RefreshPlayersList(), 1)
        end
    })

    local autoReceiverCarKeys = false
    local receiverLoopThreadCarKeys = nil
    local abilityTimerCarKeys = 0

    Tab:AddToggle("CarKeysReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Receiver (Safespot + Ability + Ride Player)",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot, uses ability, and rides selected player.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoReceiverCarKeys = Value

            if Value then
                if not SelectedPlayer or SelectedPlayer == "" then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Please select a player first!",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoReceiverCarKeys = false
                    return
                end

                if receiverLoopThreadCarKeys then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadCarKeys)
                    receiverLoopThreadCarKeys = nil
                end

                receiverLoopThreadCarKeys = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoReceiverCarKeys do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then return end

                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            abilityTimerCarKeys = abilityTimerCarKeys + 0.5
                            if abilityTimerCarKeys >= 10 then
                                local generalAbility = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                                if generalAbility then
                                    generalAbility:FireServer(false)
                                    abilityTimerCarKeys = 0
                                end
                            end

                            local targetPlayer = Players:FindFirstChild(SelectedPlayer)
                            if targetPlayer and targetPlayer.Character then
                                local targetHrp = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if targetHrp then
                                    local direction = (targetHrp.Position - hrp.Position)
                                    local distance = direction.Magnitude

                                    if distance > 10 then
                                        humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
                                        humanoid:MoveTo(targetHrp.Position)
                                        task.wait(1)
                                    else
                                        humanoid:MoveTo(hrp.Position)
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Receiver Enabled! (Safespot + Ability + Ride Player)",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if receiverLoopThreadCarKeys then
                    task.cancel(receiverLoopThreadCarKeys)
                    receiverLoopThreadCarKeys = nil
                end

                abilityTimerCarKeys = 0

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Receiver",
                    Content = "Auto Receiver Disabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Car Keys mastery."
    })

    local autoHelperCarKeys = false
    local helperLoopThreadCarKeys = nil

    Tab:AddToggle("CarKeysHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Helper (Receiver + Car Player)",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver and car player.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            autoHelperCarKeys = Value

            if Value then
                if not SelectedPlayer or SelectedPlayer == "" then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Please select a player first!",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    autoHelperCarKeys = false
                    return
                end

                if helperLoopThreadCarKeys then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopThreadCarKeys)
                    helperLoopThreadCarKeys = nil
                end

                helperLoopThreadCarKeys = task.spawn(function()
                    while autoHelperCarKeys do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if not hrp then return end

                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            task.wait(0.1)

                            local targetPlayer = Players:FindFirstChild(SelectedPlayer)
                            if targetPlayer and targetPlayer.Character then
                                local carKeys = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("CarKeysXP")
                                if carKeys and carKeys:IsA("IntValue") then
                                    local targetHrp = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetHrp then
                                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetHrp.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                                        Fluent:Notify({
                                            Title = "Car Teleport",
                                            Content = "Teleported to " .. SelectedPlayer .. "'s car!",
                                            Duration = 2
                                        })
                                    end
                                else
                                    local backpack = targetPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                                    if backpack then
                                        local carKeysInBackpack = backpack:FindFirstChild("CarKeysXP")
                                        if carKeysInBackpack and carKeysInBackpack:IsA("IntValue") then
                                            local targetHrp = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                            if targetHrp then
                                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetHrp.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end

                                    local foundCar = false
                                    for _, obj in pairs(Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                        if obj:IsA("Model") and string.find(obj.Name, SelectedPlayer) and string.find(obj.Name, "Car") then
                                            local targetPart = obj:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or
                                                obj:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                                obj:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
                                            if targetPart then
                                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPart.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                                                foundCar = true
                                                break
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Helper Enabled! (Receiver + Car Player)",
                    Duration = 3
                })

            else
                if helperLoopThreadCarKeys then
                    task.cancel(helperLoopThreadCarKeys)
                    helperLoopThreadCarKeys = nil
                end

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Helper",
                    Content = "Auto Helper Disabled!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Safespot (Once)",
        Description = "Teleports you to the safespot.",
        Callback = function()
            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if not char then return end
            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not hrp then return end

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Teleport",
                Content = "Teleported to Safespot!",
                Duration = 2
            })
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Receiver (Once)",
        Description = "Teleports you to the receiver position.",
        Callback = function()
            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if not char then return end
            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not hrp then return end

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Teleport",
                Content = "Teleported to Receiver!",
                Duration = 2
            })
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Use GeneralAbility (Once)",
        Description = "Uses the GeneralAbility remote.",
        Callback = function()
            local generalAbility = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
            if generalAbility then
                generalAbility:FireServer(false)
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Ability",
                    Content = "GeneralAbility fired with false!",
                    Duration = 2
                })
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "GeneralAbility not found!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Teleport To Car Player (Once)",
        Description = "Teleports you to the selected car player.",
        Callback = function()
            if not SelectedPlayer or SelectedPlayer == "" then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Please select a player first!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                return
            end

            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if not char then return end
            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not hrp then return end

            local targetPlayer = Players:FindFirstChild(SelectedPlayer)
            if targetPlayer and targetPlayer.Character then
                local carKeys = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("CarKeysXP")
                if carKeys and carKeys:IsA("IntValue") then
                    local targetHrp = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if targetHrp then
                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetHrp.Position + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
                        Fluent:Notify({
                            Title = "Teleport",
                            Content = "Teleported to " .. SelectedPlayer .. "'s car!",
                            Duration = 2
                        })
                    end
                else
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "No CarKeysXP found for " .. SelectedPlayer,
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Selected player not found!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    task.spawn(function()
        while true do
            task.wait(10)
            pcall(function()
                if Dropdown then
                    Dropdown:SetValues(RefreshPlayersList(), 1)
                end
            end)
        end
    end)
end

-- =================================================================================================
-- ULTRA INSTINCT TAB
-- =================================================================================================
do
    local Tab = Tabs.UltraInstinct

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "1-2 Quest",
        Content = "Quests: Hit 200 Players with Ultra Instinct, etc."
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Receiver",
        Content = "Receiver options for Ultra Instinct mastery."
    })

    local uiToggle = false

    Tab:AddToggle("UltraInstinctReceiver", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to safespot and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            uiToggle = Value

            if Value then
                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                if not safespot then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                    return false
                end

                task.spawn(function()
                    while uiToggle do
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            if char then
                                local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                    if safespot then
                                        local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                        if base then
                                            hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)

                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Ultra Instinct",
                    Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Helper",
        Content = "Helper options for Ultra Instinct mastery."
    })

    Tab:AddToggle("UltraInstinctHelper", {
        Title = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Slap Aura",
        Description = "Teleports to receiver and slaps all players.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            if Value then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while Value do
                        pcall(function()
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local char = player.Character

                            if not char or not char.Parent then
                                char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                                task.wait(1)
                            end

                            if not char then return end

                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")

                            if not hrp or not humanoid then return end

                            local glove = player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                            if glove and glove.Value ~= "Default" then
                                Fluent:Notify({
                                    Title = "Error",
                                    Content = "Equip Default Glove",
                                    Duration = 3
                                })
                                return
                            end

                            local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                            if not hasEntered then
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                end
                            else
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                            end

                            task.wait(0.5)

                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                humanoid.Health = 0
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end

                            local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                            if generalHit then
                                local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                                for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                    if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                            player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if targetPart then
                                            generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    })
end

    local ownedBadges = {}

    local function fetchOwnedBadges()
        ownedBadges = {}

        local playerData = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
        if not playerData then
            return false
        end

        local playerFolder = playerData:FindFirstChild(username)
        if not playerFolder then
            return false
        end

        local unlockedBadges = playerFolder:FindFirstChild("UnlockedBadges")
        if not unlockedBadges then
            return false
        end

        if unlockedBadges:IsA("StringValue") then
            local badgeIdsString = unlockedBadges.Value

            if badgeIdsString and badgeIdsString ~= "" then
                local trimmed = badgeIdsString:sub(2, -2)

                for id in string.gmatch(trimmed, "[^,]+") do
                    local cleanId = id:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
                    ownedBadges[cleanId] = true
                end
            end
            return true
        end
        return false
    end

    local WebhookSettings = {
        WebhookURL = "",
        SendInterval = "No time",
        LoggedObjects = {},
        SlapsThreshold = 0,
        NullShardsThreshold = 0,
        Enabled = false,
        PingType = "No Pings",
        UserID = "",
        RoleID = "",
        LastSlapsValue = 0,
        LastNullShardsValue = 0,
        TrackedSlaps = false,
        TrackedNullShards = false,
        SlapsStartValue = 0,
        NullShardsStartValue = 0,
        IsSlapsTracking = false,
        IsNullShardsTracking = false,
        ObjectLogged = {},
        SlapsLogged = false,
        NullShardsLogged = false,
        SlappleLogged = {},
        GoldenSlappleLogged = false,
        LastBadgeCheck = {},
        BadgeLogSent = false,
    }

    function WebhookSettings:GetNullShards()
        local playerData = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
        if playerData then
            local userData = playerData:FindFirstChild(username)
            if userData then
                local nullShards = userData:FindFirstChild("NullShards")
                if nullShards then
                    return nullShards.Value
                end
            end
        end
        return 0
    end

    local function getPingPrefix()
        if WebhookSettings.PingType == "No Pings" then
            return ""
        elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@User Ping" and WebhookSettings.UserID ~= "" then
            return "<@" .. WebhookSettings.UserID .. "> "
        elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@Role Ping" and WebhookSettings.RoleID ~= "" then
            return "<@&" .. WebhookSettings.RoleID .. "> "
        elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@Everyone Ping" then
            return "@everyone "
        elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@Here Ping" then
            return "@here "
        end
        return ""
    end

    local function sendWebhookMessage(content)
        if not WebhookSettings.Enabled or WebhookSettings.WebhookURL == "" then return end

        local ping = getPingPrefix()
        local fullContent = ping .. content

        local payload = {
            content = fullContent or "No message provided"
        }

        local jsonData = HttpService:JSONEncode(payload)

        local success, response = pcall(function()
            if syn and syn.request then
                return syn.request({
                    Url = WebhookSettings.WebhookURL,
                    Method = "POST",
                    Headers = {
                        ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
                    },
                    Body = jsonData
                })
            elseif http_request then
                return http_request({
                    Url = WebhookSettings.WebhookURL,
                    Method = "POST",
                    Headers = {
                        ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
                    },
                    Body = jsonData
                })
            elseif request then
                return request({
                    Url = WebhookSettings.WebhookURL,
                    Method = "POST",
                    Headers = {
                        ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
                    },
                    Body = jsonData
                })
            else
                warn("No request method available for webhook!")
                return nil, "No request method available"
            end
        end)

        if not success then
            warn("Failed to send webhook: " .. tostring(response))
        end
    end

    local function getBadgeName(badgeId)
        for _, badge in pairs(allBadges) do
            if badge.id == badgeId then
                return badge.name
            end
        end
        return "Unknown Badge"
    end

        Title = "Choose Objects Spawns To Log",
        Description = "Select objects to log when they spawn.",
        Values = {"Jet Orb", "Phase Orb", "Glitch Orb", "Siphon Orb", "MATERIALIZE Orb", "Slapple", "Golden Slapple", "Toolbox"},
        Multi = true,
        Default = {},
        Callback = function(Values)
            WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects = Values
            WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged = {}
            WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged = {}
            WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
            for _, obj in pairs(Values) do
                if obj == "Slapple" then
                    WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[obj] = {}
                elseif obj == "Golden Slapple" then
                    WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
                else
                    WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[obj] = false
                end
            end
        end
    })

        Title = "Slaps Threshold",
        Description = "Slaps amount to trigger a log.",
        Values = {"100+ Slaps", "1000+ Slaps", "10000+ Slaps", "100000+ Slaps", "1000000+ Slaps", "Custom Slaps Amount"},
        Multi = false,
        Default = 2,
        Callback = function(Value)
            if Value == "Custom Slaps Amount" then
                WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold = 0
            else
                local num = tonumber(Value:match("(%d+)")) or 0
                WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold = num
                WebhookSettings.TrackedSlaps = false
                WebhookSettings.SlapsLogged = false
            end
        end
    })

    local EnableToggle = Tab:AddToggle("WebhookEnabled", {
        Title = "Enable Webhook Logging",
        Description = "Enable or disable webhook logging.",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(value)
            if value then
                WebhookSettings.Enabled = true
                WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue = LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value
                WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue = WebhookSettings:GetNullShards()
                WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue = WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue
                WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue = WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue
                WebhookSettings.IsSlapsTracking = true
                WebhookSettings.IsNullShardsTracking = true
                WebhookSettings.SlapsLogged = false
                WebhookSettings.NullShardsLogged = false
                WebhookSettings.BadgeLogSent = false
                WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged = {}
                WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged = {}
                WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
                WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck = {}

                pcall(fetchOwnedBadges)
                for badgeId, _ in pairs(ownedBadges) do
                    WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck[badgeId] = true
                end

                for _, obj in pairs(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects) do
                    if obj == "Slapple" then
                        WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[obj] = {}
                    elseif obj == "Golden Slapple" then
                        WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
                    else
                        WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[obj] = false
                    end
                end
                sendWebhookMessage("✅ Webhook logging **STARTED**!")
            else
                sendWebhookMessage("🛑 Webhook logging **STOPPED**!")
                WebhookSettings.Enabled = false
            end
        end
    })

    -- Webhook Tracking Functions
    local function checkObjectSpawns()
        if not WebhookSettings.Enabled then return end

        local objectsToCheck = {
            ["Jet Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("JetOrb"),
            ["Phase Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("PhaseOrb"),
            ["Glitch Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("GlitchOrb"),
            ["Siphon Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("SiphonOrb"),
            ["MATERIALIZE Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("MATERIALIZEOrb"),
            ["Toolbox"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("Toolbox"),
        }

        for name, object in pairs(objectsToCheck) do
            if table.find(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects, name) then
                if object and not WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[name] then
                    WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[name] = true

                    local placeName = "Unknown"
                    pcall(function()
                        local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                        if info and info.Name then
                            placeName = info.Name
                        end
                    end)

                    local message = string.format(
                        "**From Webhook Log:**\n\n**Detected | Spawned:** %s\n\n**Name:** %s\n**Real Name:** %s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                        name, name, object.Name, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
                    )

                    sendWebhookMessage(message)
                elseif not object then
                    WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[name] = false
                end
            end
        end

        if table.find(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects, "Slapple") then
            local slapplesFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena")
            if slapplesFolder then
                local island5 = slapplesFolder:FindFirstChild("island5")
                if island5 then
                    local slapples = island5:FindFirstChild("Slapples")
                    if slapples then
                        for _, model in ipairs(slapples:GetChildren()) do
                            if model:IsA("Model") then
                                local gloveMesh = model:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                                if gloveMesh and gloveMesh:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                    local transparency = gloveMesh.Transparency
                                    local modelName = model.Name

                                    if not WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[modelName] then
                                        if transparency == 0 then
                                            WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[modelName] = true

                                            local placeName = "Unknown"
                                            pcall(function()
                                                local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                                                if info and info.Name then
                                                    placeName = info.Name
                                                end
                                            end)

                                            local message = string.format(
                                                "**From Webhook Log:**\n\n**Detected | Spawned:** Slapple\n\n**Name:** Slapple\n**Real Name:** %s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                                                modelName, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
                                            )

                                            sendWebhookMessage(message)
                                        end
                                    elseif transparency == 1 then
                                        WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[modelName] = nil
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        if table.find(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects, "Golden Slapple") then
            local slapplesFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena")
            if slapplesFolder then
                local island5 = slapplesFolder:FindFirstChild("island5")
                if island5 then
                    local slapples = island5:FindFirstChild("Slapples")
                    if slapples then
                        local goldenSlapple = slapples:FindFirstChild("GoldenSlapple")
                        if goldenSlapple and goldenSlapple:IsA("Model") then
                            local gloveMesh = goldenSlapple:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                            if gloveMesh and gloveMesh:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                local transparency = gloveMesh.Transparency

                                if transparency == 0 and not WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged then
                                    WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = true

                                    local placeName = "Unknown"
                                    pcall(function()
                                        local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                                        if info and info.Name then
                                            placeName = info.Name
                                        end
                                    end)

                                    local message = string.format(
                                        "**From Webhook Log:**\n\n**Detected | Spawned:** Golden Slapple\n\n**Name:** Golden Slapple\n**Real Name:** GoldenSlapple\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                                        placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
                                    )

                                    sendWebhookMessage(message)
                                elseif transparency == 1 then
                                    WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local function checkSlaps()
        if not WebhookSettings.Enabled or WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold == 0 or not WebhookSettings.IsSlapsTracking then return end

        local currentSlaps = LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value
        local previousSlaps = WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue

        if currentSlaps >= WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold and currentSlaps > previousSlaps then
            WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue = currentSlaps

            local earnedSlaps = currentSlaps - WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue

            local placeName = "Unknown"
            pcall(function()
                local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                if info and info.Name then
                    placeName = info.Name
                end
            end)

            local message = string.format(
                "**Slaps Counter Log**\n\n**Name:** Slaps\n**Before Amount:** %s\n**After Amount:** %s\n**Earned Total Slaps:** +%s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue, currentSlaps, earnedSlaps, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
            )

            sendWebhookMessage(message)

            WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue = currentSlaps
        end
    end

    local function checkNullShards()
        if not WebhookSettings.Enabled or WebhookSettings.NullShardsThreshold == 0 or not WebhookSettings.IsNullShardsTracking then return end

        local currentNullShards = WebhookSettings:GetNullShards()
        local previousNullShards = WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue

        if currentNullShards >= WebhookSettings.NullShardsThreshold and currentNullShards > previousNullShards then
            WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue = currentNullShards

            local earnedNullShards = currentNullShards - WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue

            local placeName = "Unknown"
            pcall(function()
                local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                if info and info.Name then
                    placeName = info.Name
                end
            end)

            local message = string.format(
                "**Null Shards Counter Log**\n\n**Name:** Null Shards\n**Before Amount:** %s\n**After Amount:** %s\n**Earned Total Null Shards:** +%s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue, currentNullShards, earnedNullShards, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
            )

            sendWebhookMessage(message)

            WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue = currentNullShards
        end
    end

    local function checkBadges()
        if not WebhookSettings.Enabled then return end

        local success = pcall(fetchOwnedBadges)
        if not success then return end

        local newBadges = {}

        for badgeId, _ in pairs(ownedBadges) do
            if not WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck[badgeId] then
                table.insert(newBadges, badgeId)
                WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck[badgeId] = true
            end
        end

        if #newBadges > 0 then
            local placeName = "Unknown"
            pcall(function()
                local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                if info and info.Name then
                    placeName = info.Name
                end
            end)

            local newBadgeNames = {}
            for _, id in pairs(newBadges) do
                for _, badge in pairs(allBadges) do
                    if badge.id == id then
                        table.insert(newBadgeNames, badge.name .. " (`" .. id .. "`)")
                        break
                    end
                end
            end

            local ownedList = {}
            for id, _ in pairs(WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck) do
                table.insert(ownedList, id)
            end

            local missingList = {}
            for _, badge in pairs(allBadges) do
                if badge.category == "GloveRewarding" and not ownedBadges[badge.id] then
                    table.insert(missingList, badge.id)
                end
            end

            local message = string.format(
                "**🎉 NEW BADGE(S) UNLOCKED!**\n\n" ..
                "**Badge(s):**\n%s\n\n" ..
                "**Place Name:** %s\n" ..
                "**Place ID:** %s\n" ..
                "**JobID:** %s\n\n" ..
                "**Total Badges Unlocked:** %s\n" ..
                "**Missing Glove Badges:** %s",
                table.concat(newBadgeNames, "\n"),
                placeName,
                game.PlaceId,
                game.JobId,
                #ownedList > 0 and #ownedList .. " badges" or "None",
                #missingList > 0 and #missingList .. " badges" or "None"
            )

            sendWebhookMessage(message)
        end
    end

    local function startWebhookLoop()
        while true do
            if WebhookSettings.Enabled then
                pcall(checkObjectSpawns)
                pcall(checkSlaps)
                pcall(checkNullShards)
                pcall(checkBadges)
            end

            local waitTime = 1
            if WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "30 Seconds" then
                waitTime = 30
            elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "1 Minute" then
                waitTime = 60
            elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "10 Minutes" then
                waitTime = 600
            elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "30 Minutes" then
                waitTime = 1800
            elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "1 Hour" then
                waitTime = 3600
            elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "5 Hours" then
                waitTime = 18000
            elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "10 Hours" then
                waitTime = 36000
            elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "1 Day" then
                waitTime = 86400
            end

            task.wait(waitTime)
        end
    end

    task.spawn(startWebhookLoop)
end

    local Tab = Tabs.Settings

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Value Changer",
        Content = "Change visual values."
    })

    local SlapChanger = nil
    Tab:AddInput("SlapChanger", {
        Title = "How Many Slaps? (Visual)",
        Description = "Enter the number of slaps you want to set.",
        Default = "",
        Placeholder = "e.g., 1000000",
        Numeric = true,
        Finished = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            local slapNumber = tonumber(Value)
            if slapNumber and slapNumber > 0 then
                SlapChanger = slapNumber
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Type a correct number (greater than 0)!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Set Slaps (Visual)",
        Description = "Sets your slaps to the entered value.",
        Callback = function()
            if SlapChanger then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value = SlapChanger
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Please enter a valid number of slaps!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    local nullshardChanger = nil
    Tab:AddInput("NullShardChanger", {
        Title = "How Many Null Shards? (Visual)",
        Description = "Enter the number of Null Shards you want to set.",
        Default = "",
        Placeholder = "e.g., 1000",
        Numeric = true,
        Finished = false,
        Callback = function(Value)
            local nullshardNumber = tonumber(Value)
            if nullshardNumber and nullshardNumber >= 0 then
                getgenv().nullshardChanger = tostring(nullshardNumber)
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Type a correct number (0 or greater)!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Set Null Shards (Visual)",
        Description = "Sets your Null Shards to the entered value.",
        Callback = function()
            if getgenv().nullshardChanger then
                local playerName = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name

                local playerData = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("PlayerData", 5)
                if not playerData then
                    return
                end

                local playerFolder = playerData:WaitForChild(playerName, 5)
                if not playerFolder then
                    return
                end

                local nullShardsValue = playerFolder:WaitForChild("NullShards", 5)
                if not nullShardsValue then
                    return
                end

                if nullShardsValue.ClassName ~= "StringValue" then
                    return
                end

                local oldValue = nullShardsValue.Value
                nullShardsValue.Value = getgenv().nullshardChanger

                print("[Null Shards] Changed from " .. oldValue .. " to " .. getgenv().nullshardChanger)
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Please enter a valid number first!",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    })

    Tab:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Stuff Giver",
        Content = "Give badges and emotes."
    })

    Tab:AddButton({
        Title = "Give All Badges (Visual)",

        end
